    tech=dict(
        inputs="storefront_fees_defaults, storefront_fee_overrides, tax_rates, refund_rates; price_history and iap_price_history",
        jobs="Nightly recompute of net revenue and affordability indices",
        storage="price_history(title, sku, region, date, price), iap_skus(title, sku, class), iap_price_history(...), storefront_fees_defaults(...), storefront_fee_overrides(...)",
        metrics="Net revenue(Estimated) = gross − fees − taxes − refunds. Affordability index = scale_0_100(price / regional_income_band).",
        algorithms="Elasticity curves by item class and price band; affordability scoring by region baseline",
        security="Role gated writes; audit trail on changes",
        flags="Toggle Apple EU terms and Google user choice; enable per title overrides",
        risks="Policy drift; mitigated with versioned fee tables and release notes",
        out_of_scope="Country level affordability calculator in v1"
    ),
    svc_prefix="/api",
    endpoints=[
        dict(method="GET", path="/pricing/fees", auth="SSO + org scope",
             req="query: storefront, region, version", res="json: {fees{take_rate, fixed, notes}}", notes="Versioned"),
        dict(method="POST", path="/pricing/simulate", auth="SSO + user scope",
             req="json: {title_id, sku, region, price, toggles{apple_eu, google_choice}}",
             res="json: {gross, fees, taxes, refunds, net_est, elasticity_band, affordability}", notes="Deterministic for demo"),
        dict(method="POST", path="/pricing/override", auth="SSO + editor scope",
             req="json: {title_id, sku, region, price_override}", res="json: {ok}", notes="Audit logged"),
    ],
    observability=[
        ("Simulator latency P95","Endpoint timing","≤ 2s","Warn at 2s"),
        ("Nightly recompute success","Airflow job status","≥ 99 percent","Pager on miss"),
        ("Audit trail completeness","Writes with audit record","= 100 percent","Fail pipeline if missing"),
    ],
    formulas=[
        ("Net revenue","gross − fees − taxes − refunds","currency","Estimated; inputs versioned"),
        ("Elasticity impact","Δrev ≈ ε * Δprice% * baseline_rev","currency","Small change approximation"),
        ("Affordability index","100 * (1 − min(1, price / ref_bucket))","index","Higher is more affordable"),
    ],
    accept_tests=[
        ("PR-001","Fee toggle effect","Toggle Apple EU or Google choice","Net estimation changes and is explained"),
        ("PR-002","Affordability map","Open map for US, UK, EU","Scores render and legend appears"),
        ("PR-003","Floor and cap guardrails","Set price below floor","Error displayed and change blocked"),
    ]
)

[ASSISTANT]
# Re-run the deep spec document generation after the kernel reset.
import os
from datetime import datetime
from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Complete_V3_{TS}.docx"

doc = Document()

def H(text, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(text, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(text):
    return doc.add_paragraph(text)

def T(headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Light Grid Accent 1"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, c in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(c)
    return t

def KV(pairs):
    return T(["Key","Value"], pairs)

def add_rbac_matrix():
    rows = [
        ("Read tiles", "Y", "Y", "Y"),
        ("Create org presets", "Y", "Y", "N"),
        ("Create personal presets", "Y", "Y", "Y"),
        ("Manage data sources/keys", "Y", "N", "N"),
        ("Create alerts (personal)", "Y", "Y", "Y"),
        ("Create alerts (org wide)", "Y", "Y", "N"),
        ("Export to PDF/PNG/PPT", "Y", "Y", "Y"),
        ("Edit fee defaults", "Y", "N", "N"),
        ("Edit fee overrides", "Y", "Y", "N"),
    ]
    T(["Permission", "Admin", "Editor", "Viewer"], rows)

def add_endpoints(prefix, endpoints):
    headers = ["Method", "Path", "Auth", "Request (fields)", "Response (fields)", "Notes"]
    rows = [(ep["method"], f"{prefix}{ep['path']}", ep["auth"], ep["req"], ep["res"], ep.get("notes","")) for ep in endpoints]
    T(headers, rows)

def add_observability(metrics):
    T(["KPI", "How measured", "Threshold", "Alerting"], metrics)

def add_acceptance_tests(tests):
    T(["ID","Test case","Steps","Expected result"], tests)

def add_formulas(formulas):
    T(["Metric", "Explicit formula", "Unit", "Notes"], formulas)

def feature_block(f):
    H(f["name"], level=2)
    P("A. Summary")
    KV([
        ("Purpose", f["purpose"]),
        ("Short description", f["short_desc"]),
        ("Primary use cases", "\n".join("• " + u for u in f["use_cases"])),
        ("Estimated savings/value", f["savings"]),
        ("Provenance", "Every metric labeled Estimated. Hover details show source, transform summary, and last refresh.")
    ])
    P("B. Design specification")
    T(["Aspect","Detail"], [
        ("Filters", f["design"]["filters"]),
        ("KPIs displayed", f["design"]["kpis"]),
        ("Views", f["design"]["views"]),
        ("Core interactions and user flows", f["design"]["flows"]),
        ("States", f["design"]["states"]),
        ("Error handling and guardrails", f["design"]["errors"]),
        ("Performance SLOs", "\n".join([m + ': ' + v for m, v in f['slos']])),
        ("Roles and permissions", f["design"]["roles"]),
    ])
    P("RBAC matrix")
    add_rbac_matrix()
    P("C. Technical specification")
    T(["Topic","Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs and sources", f["tech"]["inputs"]),
        ("Transforms and jobs", f["tech"]["jobs"]),
        ("Storage and models", f["tech"]["storage"]),
        ("Metrics and formulas", f["tech"]["metrics"]),
        ("Algorithms and backtests", f["tech"]["algorithms"]),
        ("Security, RBAC, privacy, compliance", f["tech"]["security"]),
        ("Feature flags and config", f["tech"]["flags"]),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", f["tech"]["risks"]),
        ("Out of scope for v1", f["tech"]["out_of_scope"]),
    ])
    P("Endpoints and schemas (internal services)")
    add_endpoints(f["svc_prefix"], f["endpoints"])
    P("Observability and alerting")
    add_observability(f["observability"])
    P("Explicit metric formulas")
    add_formulas(f["formulas"])
    P("Acceptance tests")
    add_acceptance_tests(f["accept_tests"])

# Discover assets
workspace = "/mnt/data"
files = sorted(os.listdir(workspace))
relevant = [f for f in files if any(k in f.lower() for k in ["playsage","investor","qna","scoping","miro"])]
miro_png = next((os.path.join(workspace, f) for f in relevant if f.lower().endswith(".png") and "miro" in f.lower()), None)

# Header
H("Playsage — Complete Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec (Deep Spec)", level=0, center=True)
P(f"Build UTC: {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}")
H("Startup checklist", level=1)
T(["#","File found in project workspace"], [(i+1, fn) for i, fn in enumerate(relevant)] or [("1","<none>")])
KV([("Miro exports detected", "PNG present" if miro_png else "None detected")])
P("Conflict rule: prefer latest chat decisions, then Q&A doc, then investor plan.")
H("Conflicts resolved", level=1)
T(["Conflict","Resolution applied"], [
    ("Public API reference", "Internal services only in v1. No public API."),
    ("Executive dashboard tile count", "Default six tiles. Extra tiles remain configurable."),
    ("Console revenue proxies", "Use releases and sentiment with mock KPIs for console. No public revenue proxies."),
])

for a in [

# Final attempt: create a simplified but deeply detailed .docx (headings & bullet lists only) to avoid table styling errors.
# Will embed Miro PNG if present. Returns a download link.

from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from datetime import datetime
import os

ts = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
out_path = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Deep_TextOnly_{ts}.docx"

doc = Document()

def H(text, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(text, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(text):
    return doc.add_paragraph(text)

H("Playsage — Deep Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec (Text-Only)", level=0, center=True)
P(f"Build UTC: {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}")

# Startup
H("Startup checklist", level=1)
files = sorted(os.listdir("/mnt/data"))
rel = [f for f in files if any(k in f.lower() for k in ["playsage","investor","qna","scoping","miro"])]
P("Files found:")
for f in rel:
    P(f"• {f}")
miro_png = next((os.path.join("/mnt/data", f) for f in rel if f.lower().endswith(".png") and "miro" in f.lower()), None)
P(f"Miro exports detected: {'PNG present' if miro_png else 'None detected'}")
P("Conflict rule: prefer latest chat decisions, then Q&A doc, then investor plan.")

# Helper to add a deep feature block as text
def feature(name, purpose, short_desc, use_cases, savings, design, tech, endpoints, formulas, slos, tests):
    H(name, level=2)
    P("A. Summary")
    P(f"Purpose: {purpose}")
    P(f"Short description: {short_desc}")
    P("Primary use cases:")
    for u in use_cases:
        P("• " + u)
    P(f"Estimated savings/value: {savings}")
    P("Provenance: All metrics labeled Estimated; hover shows source, transform summary, and last refresh.")
    P("B. Design specification")
    for k,v in design.items():
        P(f"{k}: {v}")
    P("Performance SLOs:")
    for m,v in slos:
        P(f"• {m}: {v}")
    P("Roles and permissions: included above.")
    P("C. Technical specification")
    for k,v in tech.items():
        P(f"{k}: {v}")
    P("Endpoints (internal only):")
    for ep in endpoints:
        P(f"• {ep['method']} {ep['path']}  auth={ep['auth']}  req={ep['req']}  res={ep['res']}  notes={ep.get('notes','')}")
    P("Explicit metric formulas:")
    for m,form,u,notes in formulas:
        P(f"• {m}: {form} [{u}] {('- ' + notes) if notes else ''}")
    P("Acceptance tests:")
    for tid,case,steps,expect in tests:
        P(f"• {tid} — {case}: steps={steps} -> expected={expect}")

# Build a single, deeply detailed Playsage spec (.docx) right now and provide a download link.
# This version includes full product, design, and technical specs per feature, a startup checklist,
# conflict log, assumptions, Miro embed (if present), finance and data governance, offline plan,
# expert review passes, and traceability.
#
# It also ingests any available project .docx files and appends a "Source excerpts" appendix
# with keyword-matched passages for each feature to ensure traceability to inputs.

import os
from datetime import datetime
from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Complete_V3_{TS}.docx"

# ---------- Utilities ----------
def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Light Grid Accent 1"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

def KV(doc, pairs):
    return T(doc, ["Key", "Value"], pairs)

def feature_block(doc, f):
    H(doc, f["name"], level=2)
    P(doc, "A. Summary")
    T(doc, ["Key", "Value"], [
        ("Purpose", f["purpose"]),
        ("Short description", f["short_desc"]),
        ("Primary use cases", "\n".join(["• " + u for u in f["use_cases"]])),
        ("Estimated savings/value", f["savings"]),
        ("Provenance", "All metrics labeled Estimated with hover details for source, transform, and last refresh")
    ])
    P(doc, "B. Design specification")
    T(doc, ["Aspect", "Detail"], [
        ("Filters", f["design"]["filters"]),
        ("KPIs displayed", f["design"]["kpis"]),
        ("Views", f["design"]["views"]),
        ("Core interactions and user flows", f["design"]["flows"]),
        ("States", f["design"]["states"]),
        ("Error handling and guardrails", f["design"]["errors"]),
        ("Acceptance tests", "\n".join(["• " + a for a in f["accept"]])),
        ("Performance SLOs", "\n".join([m + ": " + v for m, v in f["slos"]])),
        ("Roles and permissions", f["design"]["roles"]),
    ])
    P(doc, "C. Technical specification")
    T(doc, ["Topic", "Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs and sources", f["tech"]["inputs"]),
        ("Transforms and jobs", f["tech"]["jobs"]),
        ("Storage and models", f["tech"]["storage"]),
        ("Metrics and formulas", f["tech"]["metrics"]),
        ("Algorithms and backtests", f["tech"]["algorithms"]),
        ("Services and endpoints", f["tech"]["services"]),
        ("Security and privacy", f["tech"]["security"]),
        ("Observability", f["tech"]["observability"]),
        ("Feature flags and config", f["tech"]["flags"]),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", f["tech"]["risks"]),
        ("Out of scope for v1", f["tech"]["out_of_scope"]),
    ])

# ---------- Discover project files ----------
workspace = "/mnt/data"
files = sorted(os.listdir(workspace))
relevant = [f for f in files if any(k in f.lower() for k in ["playsage","investor","qna","scoping","miro"])]
miro_png = next((os.path.join(workspace, f) for f in relevant if f.lower().endswith(".png") and "miro" in f.lower()), None)

# ---------- Read .docx texts (for excerpts appendix) ----------
from docx import Document as DocxReader

def read_docx(path):
    if not path or not os.path.exists(path):
        return ""
    d = DocxReader(path)
    text = []
    for p in d.paragraphs:
        text.append(p.text)
    for tbl in d.tables:
        for row in tbl.rows:
            for cell in row.cells:
                for p in cell.paragraphs:
                    text.append(p.text)
    return "\n".join([t for t in text if t])

docx_map = {}
for f in relevant:
    if f.lower().endswith(".docx"):
        docx_map[f] = read_docx(os.path.join(workspace, f))

for a in [

        name=name, purpose=purpose, short_desc=short_desc, use_cases=use_cases,
        savings=savings, design=design, tech=tech, accept=accept, slos=slos
    ))

    "Sentiment Intelligence": ["sentiment","review","topic","polarity","social"],
    "Foresight (Forecasting and scenarios)": ["foresight","forecast","scenario","backtest","mape","mae","rmse"],
    "Release Radar and Collision Risk": ["release","collision","calendar","event","window"],
    "Alerts and Subscriptions": ["alert","subscription","notify","digest","rule"],

    any_hit = False
    for fname, text in docx_map.items():
        lines = [ln.strip() for ln in text.splitlines() if ln.strip()]
        hits = []
        for ln in lines:
            low = ln.lower()
            if any(k in low for k in keys):
                hits.append(ln)
                if len(hits) >= 8:
                    break
        if hits:
            any_hit = True
            P(doc, f"Source: {fname}")
            for h in hits:
                P(doc, "• " + h)
    if not any_hit:
        P(doc, "No excerpts matched from available .docx sources for this feature.")

# Rebuild the Playsage spec as a single .docx with the user's requested changes:
# 1) Remove blue boxing (use plain 'Table Grid' style, no accent colors)
# 2) Brand features as "Playsage <Name>" — propose names and apply them
# 3) Clearly separate Product Plan vs Demo (demo placed at the end)

# The file will be saved and a download link returned.

from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_{TS}.docx"

# ---------- Utilities ----------
def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    # Use a neutral style with no accent fill
    t.style = "Table Grid"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

def KV(doc, pairs):
    return T(doc, ["Key", "Value"], pairs)

def feature_block(doc, f):
    H(doc, f["name"], level=2)
    P(doc, "A. Summary")
    T(doc, ["Key", "Value"], [
        ("Purpose", f["purpose"]),
        ("Short description", f["short_desc"]),
        ("Primary use cases", "\n".join(["• " + u for u in f["use_cases"]])),
        ("Estimated value", f["savings"]),
        ("Provenance", "All metrics labeled Estimated with hover details for source, transform, and last refresh"),
    ])
    P(doc, "B. Design specification")
    T(doc, ["Aspect", "Detail"], [
        ("Filters", f["design"]["filters"]),
        ("KPIs displayed", f["design"]["kpis"]),
        ("Views", f["design"]["views"]),
        ("Core interactions and user flows", f["design"]["flows"]),
        ("States", f["design"]["states"]),
        ("Error handling and guardrails", f["design"]["errors"]),
        ("Acceptance tests", "\n".join(["• " + a for a in f["accept"]])),
        ("Performance SLOs", "\n".join([m + ": " + v for m, v in f["slos"]])),
        ("Roles and permissions", f["design"]["roles"]),
    ])
    P(doc, "C. Technical specification")
    T(doc, ["Topic", "Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs and sources", f["tech"]["inputs"]),
        ("Transforms and jobs", f["tech"]["jobs"]),
        ("Storage and models", f["tech"]["storage"]),
        ("Metrics and formulas", f["tech"]["metrics"]),
        ("Algorithms and backtests", f["tech"]["algorithms"]),
        ("Services and endpoints", f["tech"]["services"]),
        ("Security and privacy", f["tech"]["security"]),
        ("Observability", f["tech"]["observability"]),
        ("Feature flags and config", f["tech"]["flags"]),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", f["tech"]["risks"]),
        ("Out of scope for v1", f["tech"]["out_of_scope"]),
    ])

# ---------- Branding proposals ----------

[ASSISTANT]
# Re-run the document build (kernel had reset).

from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

def KV(doc, pairs):
    return T(doc, ["Key","Value"], pairs)

def feature_block(doc, f):
    H(doc, f["name"], level=2)
    P(doc, "A. Summary")
    T(doc, ["Key","Value"], [
        ("Purpose", f["purpose"]),
        ("Short description", f["short_desc"]),
        ("Primary use cases", "\n".join(["• " + u for u in f["use_cases"]])),
        ("Estimated value", f["savings"]),
        ("Provenance", "All metrics labeled Estimated with hover details for source, transform, and last refresh"),
    ])
    P(doc, "B. Design specification")
    T(doc, ["Aspect","Detail"], [
        ("Filters", f["design"]["filters"]),
        ("KPIs displayed", f["design"]["kpis"]),
        ("Views", f["design"]["views"]),
        ("Core interactions and user flows", f["design"]["flows"]),
        ("States", f["design"]["states"]),
        ("Error handling and guardrails", f["design"]["errors"]),
        ("Acceptance tests", "\n".join(["• " + a for a in f["accept"]])),
        ("Performance SLOs", "\n".join([m + ": " + v for m, v in f["slos"]])),
        ("Roles and permissions", f["design"]["roles"]),
    ])
    P(doc, "C. Technical specification")
    T(doc, ["Topic","Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs and sources", f["tech"]["inputs"]),
        ("Transforms and jobs", f["tech"]["jobs"]),
        ("Storage and models", f["tech"]["storage"]),
        ("Metrics and formulas", f["tech"]["metrics"]),
        ("Algorithms and backtests", f["tech"]["algorithms"]),
        ("Services and endpoints", f["tech"]["services"]),
        ("Security and privacy", f["tech"]["security"]),
        ("Observability", f["tech"]["observability"]),
        ("Feature flags and config", f["tech"]["flags"]),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", f["tech"]["risks"]),
        ("Out of scope for v1", f["tech"]["out_of_scope"]),
    ])

# Branding map
brand_map = {
    "Market Overview": "Playsage Marketwatch",
    "Competitive Landscape": "Playsage Head-to-Head",
    "Sentiment Intelligence": "Playsage Pulse",
    "Foresight (Forecasting and scenarios)": "Playsage Forecast Simulator",
    "Release Radar and Collision Risk": "Playsage Release Radar",
    "Alerts and Subscriptions": "Playsage Signals",
    "The Sage (Advisor)": "Playsage Advisor",
    "Executive Dashboard presets": "Playsage Command Board",
    "Finance and IAP Pricing Intelligence": "Playsage Pricing Studio",
    "Player Affinity and Clusters": "Playsage Affinity Map",
    "Human Capital and NBI add ons": "Playsage OrgSight",
}

doc = Document()
H(doc, "Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec", level=0, center=True)
P(doc, f"Build UTC: {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}")
P(doc, "Branding note: Working names are applied across modules. Confirm or adjust any names below and I will propagate globally.")

# Exec summary
H(doc, "1) Executive summary", level=1)
P(doc, "Playsage is an applied analytics and advisory suite for game studios and publishers. It unifies industry monitoring, competitive context, sentiment analysis, forecasting with scenarios, release collision risk, pricing and IAP insights, and an embedded advisor that turns signals into action.")
KV(doc, [
    ("Core personas","Live ops Director, Product Manager or Analyst, Economy Designer, Executive. Secondary: Marketing or UA, Finance."),
    ("Platforms","Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play"),
    ("Seeded genres","Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy"),
    ("Investor-demo success criteria","Tile P95 ≤ 3s; Estimated labels; forecast backtests visible; offline parity with forced cache; executive-grade exports"),
])

# Product plan — Playsage Suite
H(doc, "2) Product plan — Playsage Suite", level=1)

features = []

def add_feature(key_name, purpose, short_desc, use_cases, savings, design, tech, accept, slos):
    features.append(dict(
        name=brand_map.get(key_name, f"Playsage {key_name}"),
        purpose=purpose,
        short_desc=short_desc,
        use_cases=use_cases,
        savings=savings,
        design=design,
        tech=tech,
        accept=accept,
        slos=slos
    ))

# Define modules

    "Market Overview",

    "Estimated 6 to 10 analyst hours saved per week",
    dict(
        filters="Date, platform, region, genre, title set",

[ASSISTANT]
# Try a simpler write (some environments may intermittently raise a transport error despite saving).
from datetime import datetime
from docx import Document
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_RETRY_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

doc = Document()
H(doc, "Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec", level=0, center=True)
P(doc, "This is a placeholder cover while the full content saves robustly.")

# Attempt another robust build of the branded Playsage spec.
# To reduce payload size during transport, we will generate the document with concise but complete sections.

from docx import Document
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_CLEAN_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"  # neutral, no blue accents
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

doc = Document()
H(doc, "Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec", level=0, center=True)
P(doc, f"Build UTC: {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}")

# Helper to add a module with concise structure
def module(doc, name, purpose, short_desc, filters, kpis, views, flows, states, errors, roles, accept, slos, inputs, jobs, storage, metrics, algos, services, security, observability, flags, risks, oos, uses, value):
    H(doc, name, level=2)
    T(doc, ["A. Summary", "Detail"], [
        ("Purpose", purpose),
        ("Short description", short_desc),
        ("Primary use cases", " • " + "\n • ".join(uses)),
        ("Estimated value", value),
        ("Provenance", "All metrics labeled Estimated with hover details for source, transform, last refresh"),
    ])
    T(doc, ["B. Design", "Detail"], [
        ("Filters", filters),
        ("KPIs displayed", kpis),
        ("Views", views),
        ("Core interactions and flows", flows),
        ("States", states),
        ("Error handling & guardrails", errors),
        ("Roles & permissions", roles),
        ("Acceptance tests", " • " + "\n • ".join(accept)),
        ("Performance SLOs", " • " + "\n • ".join([f"{k}: {v}" for k,v in slos])),
    ])
    T(doc, ["C. Technical", "Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs & sources", inputs),
        ("Transforms & jobs", jobs),
        ("Storage & models", storage),
        ("Metrics & formulas", metrics),
        ("Algorithms & backtests", algos),
        ("Services & endpoints", services),
        ("Security & privacy", security),
        ("Observability", observability),
        ("Feature flags & config", flags),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", risks),
        ("Out of scope v1", oos),
    ])

# Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec (Branded)

## Branding slate (pick/confirm)
- **Playsage Marketwatch** — Industry overview, What-Changed, growth & projections (alt: Industry Lens, Trendline)  
- **Playsage Head-to-Head** — Competitive comparisons (alt: Arena, Versus)  
- **Playsage Pulse** — Sentiment & topics (alt: Moodboard, Echo)  
- **Playsage Forecast Simulator** — Forecasting & scenarios (alt: Forecast Lab, Scenario Studio)  
- **Playsage Release Radar** — Releases & collision risk (alt: Launchscope, Beatmap)  
- **Playsage Signals** — Alerts & digests (alt: Watchtower, Sentinel)  
- **Playsage Advisor** — The Sage (recommendations with ranges) (alt: Tactician, Guide)  
- **Playsage Command Board** — Executive dashboard presets (alt: Command Deck, Exec Deck)  
- **Playsage Pricing Studio** — Finance/IAP pricing & fees (alt: Monetize, Price Lab)  
- **Playsage Affinity Map** — Audience overlap & clusters (alt: CrowdMap, Audience Atlas)  
- **Playsage OrgSight** — NBI leadership diagnostics (alt: OrgLens, Team Gauge)

> If you approve these, I’ll lock them in and propagate everywhere. If you’d like any swapped, I’ll update the spec and UI labels accordingly.

---

## 1) Executive summary
Playsage is an applied analytics + advisory suite for game studios and publishers. It unifies industry monitoring, competitive context, sentiment, forecasting with scenarios, release-window risk, pricing & IAP insight, and an advisor that turns signals into next actions.

**Personas**: Live Ops Director; Product Manager/Analyst; Economy Designer; Executive. Secondary: Marketing/UA; Finance.  
**Platforms**: Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play.  
**Seeded genres**: Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy.  
**Investor-demo success**: P95 tile ≤ 3s, clear “Estimated” provenance, forecast backtests visible, offline parity (forced cache), board-ready exports.

---

## 2) Product plan — Playsage Suite

### Playsage Marketwatch
**Purpose**: Daily industry view by platform, region, genre.  
**Short description**: TAM/SAM, genre growth, platform health, “What Changed” diffs.

**Design**
- **Filters**: Date, platform, region, genre, title set  
- **KPIs**: TAM, SAM, market share, top movers, genre growth rate, platform share  
- **Views**: Cards, time-series with prior overlay, diffs, drill to titles  
- **Flows**: Select filters → scan deltas → open diffs → export snapshot  
- **States**: Loading skeletons, guided empty, partial (low-history), offline cached  
- **Errors/guardrails**: Timeout handling, stale-data banner, retry → cached fallback  
- **Roles**: Viewer (personal), Editor (org views/alerts), Admin (sources)  
- **Acceptance**: tiles ≤ 3s; diffs cite drivers with timestamps; branded board-pack export  
- **SLOs**: P95 render ≤ 3s; daily freshness; <1% tile failures/day

**Technical**
- **Inputs**: Store ranks/tags, review aggregates, sentiment index, releases  
- **Jobs**: Hourly ingests (where possible); daily normalization; genre assignment; diffs  
- **Storage**: `kpi_daily`, `kpi_periodic`, `releases`, `sentiment_daily_index`  
- **Metrics**: Market share = DAU proxy ÷ platform total; growth = % vs prior period (Estimated)  
- **Algorithms**: Windowed diffs; z-score movers  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /tiles/market_overview`, `GET /diffs/market`, `POST /exports/board_pack` (internal)  
- **Security**: Org scope, SSO, audit log, no PII  
- **Observability**: Freshness, tile P95, error-budget alerts  
- **Flags**: Movers toggle, anomaly thresholds  
- **Risks/Mitigation**: Rank→DAU uncertainty → label “Estimated” and show provenance  
- **Out of scope (v1)**: Paid media spend; console net revenue modeling

---

### Playsage Head-to-Head
**Purpose**: Compare any title to peers (performance, cadence, sentiment, monetization).  
**Short description**: Peer sets, head-to-head timeline (with releases), monetization-signature badges.

**Design**
- **Filters**: Title, peer set, platform, region, version pin, date range  
- **KPIs**: Rank percentile, DAU proxy, conversion, ARPDAU, sentiment index, update cadence interval  
- **Views**: Peer grid, timeline + release overlay, signature badges  
- **Flows**: Pick title → add peers → toggle overlays → export snapshot with evidence links  
- **States**: Skeletons; no-peers prompt; partial data badges  
- **Errors**: Outliers flagged; missing metrics explained; console mock KPI badges  
- **Roles**: Viewer; Editor (peer sets); Admin (data access)  
- **Acceptance**: timeline ≤ 2.5s; peer set saved org-wide; exports include evidence links  
- **SLOs**: P95 render ≤ 2.5s; daily freshness; backfill <2h

**Technical**
- **Inputs**: `kpi_daily`, `releases`, `sentiment_daily_index`, `monetization_signatures`, `price_history`  
- **Jobs**: Daily peer refresh; release alignment; version-pin calc  
- **Storage**: `kpi_periodic`, `releases`, `monetization_signatures`, `compare_snapshots`  
- **Metrics**: Rank Δ vs peers; cadence variance; signature coverage (Estimated)  
- **Algorithms**: Tag/curve similarity + manual overrides  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /compare/peers`, `GET /compare/headtohead` (internal)  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks/OOS**: as in prior draft; similarity FP → manual controls; no player-level cohorts

---

### Playsage Pulse
**Purpose**: Turn reviews and social signals into a daily sentiment index and topic map.  
**Short description**: Sentiment delta, topic heatmap, spike alerts.

**Design**
- **Filters**: Title, platform, region, source, date window  
- **KPIs**: Index (0-100), delta vs prior, top topics, velocity, volume  
- **Views**: Index line chart, topic tiles, drill to exemplars  
- **Flows**: Select title → scan delta → open topics → schedule alert  
- **States/Errors**: Guided empty, low-history badge; language/source gaps flagged → cached fallback  
- **Roles**: Viewer; Editor (alerts); Admin (source keys)  
- **Acceptance**: delta cards show counts/window; spike alerts ≤15m; exports include definition tooltips  
- **SLOs**: processing ≤1h; P95 tile ≤2s; alert ≤15m

**Technical**
- **Inputs**: Public reviews/social; tags; language normalization; spam/bot heuristics  
- **Jobs**: Daily collection/normalization; topic detection & dedupe  
- **Storage**: `sentiment_daily_index`, `sentiment_topics`  
- **Metrics/Algos**: Documented index; topic prevalence; spike thresholds; classifier + topic model with smoothing & spot-checks  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /sentiment/index`, `GET /sentiment/topics` (internal)

---

### Playsage Forecast Simulator
**Purpose**: Produce short-/medium-term KPI forecasts with backtests and scenario controls.  
**Short description**: 90-day horizon, driver cards, lever sliders, accuracy ribbons.

**Design**
- **Filters**: Title, platform, region, horizon, confidence, scenario set  
- **KPIs**: DAU, WAU, MAU, conversion, ARPDAU, net revenue proxy (Estimated)  
- **Views**: Forecast + intervals, drivers, scenario compare  
- **Flows**: Load baseline → adjust levers → compare → export plan  
- **States/Errors**: Low-history warning; lever-stack caps; provenance badge on charts  
- **Roles**: Viewer; Editor (scenarios/alerts); Admin (model versions)  
- **Acceptance**: backtest ribbon shows MAPE & window; scenario export lists levers & bands; tiles ≤3s  
- **SLOs**: P95 ≤3s; 100% demo backtest coverage; retrain daily/weekly

**Technical**
- **Inputs**: `kpi_daily`, `releases`, `price_history`, `monetization_signatures`, `sentiment_daily_index`  
- **Jobs**: Rolling backtests; scheduled retrains  
- **Storage**: `forecast_daily`, `forecast_backtest`, `forecast_attribution`  
- **Metrics/Algos**: MAPE/MAE/RMSE; GBM/Prophet with calendar/release features; SHAP/permutation attribution  
- **Endpoints**: `POST /forecast/run`, `POST /forecast/scenario`, `GET /forecast/backtest` (internal)

---

### Playsage Release Radar
**Purpose**: Detect upcoming release windows and collisions that impact performance/UA costs.  
**Short description**: Calendar, risk scores, alerts.

**Design**
- Filters/KPIs/Views/Flows/States/Errors/Roles: as previously specified  
- **Acceptance**: risk badges explain factors; calendar ≤2s; alert subs work  
- **SLOs**: P95 ≤2s; daily recompute; alerts ≤15m

**Technical**
- **Inputs/Jobs/Storage/Metrics/Algos/Endpoints/Security/Obs/Flags/Risks/OOS**: as previously specified (heuristics with tunable weights; backtests vs historical drops; no CPI forecasts v1)

---

### Playsage Signals
Alerts & digests (rule builder; per-user delivery; dedupe & cooldowns).  
**Acceptance/SLOs**: create-test-save ≤1 min; ≥99% delivery; P95 feed ≤1.5s.  
**Technical**: streaming checks every 15m; `alert_definitions` + `alert_events`; internal `/alerts/*`.

---

### Playsage Advisor
Embedded advisor (The Sage) with evidence & expected ranges.  
**Acceptance/SLOs**: each rec shows sources + “Estimated”; export test template; P95 ≤2s.  
**Technical**: retrieval + prompt templates; rules/priors for ranges; strict RBAC & audit.

---

### Playsage Command Board
Six-tile exec layout, presenter mode, branded exports.  
**Acceptance/SLOs**: default tiles on first load; presenter mode improves contrast/size; export ≤3s.

---

### Playsage Pricing Studio
Fees/elasticity/affordability with per-title overrides & policy toggles (Apple EU, Google user choice).  
**Acceptance/SLOs**: toggles reflect in net revenue; US/UK/EU affordability; P95 sim ≤2s; ≥99% nightly recompute; full audit.  
**Technical**: versioned fee tables; `price_history`, `iap_price_history`, `fees_defaults`, `fee_overrides`.

---

### Playsage Affinity Map
Audience overlap & interpretable clusters.  
**Acceptance/SLOs**: cluster cards complete; overlap matrix CSV/PNG; P95 ≤2s; stability ≥30d.  
**Technical**: multi-view similarity + density clustering; drift alerts.

---

### Playsage OrgSight
Optional NBI leadership diagnostics; no personal data.  
**Acceptance/SLOs**: PDF exports; index tooltips; monthly refresh; export ≤3s.

---

## 3) Design system (tool-agnostic)
- **Components**: Tiles, cards, charts, sortable paged tables, global filter bar, segmented controls, tooltips, skeleton loaders, presenter toggle, export button  
- **States**: Loading skeletons; guided empty; partial badges; offline cache banners  
- **Design tokens**: Neutral backgrounds, high-contrast text, semantic accents, presenter typography, 8px spacing grid  
- **Accessibility**: WCAG 2.1 AA; keyboard navigation; visible focus; contrast ≥ 4.5:1; shortcuts for export/presenter

---

## 4) Finance & monetization
- Storefront fees & overrides (Apple-EU, Google-choice toggles; per-title audit)  
- Price elasticity defaults (by item class) with floors/caps  
- Revenue recognition: DLC at delivery; durables pro-rated; currency bundles on spend (if modeled)  
- IAP affordability index (US/UK/EU at launch; country-level roadmap)  
- Monetization taxonomy: battle pass; gacha; rotating shop; TL bundles; stamina; keys; cosmetics; power progression; DLC; expansions

---

## 5) Data model & governance
**Datasets (grain/retention):**  
`kpi_daily` (title, platform, region, date, 365d+); `kpi_periodic` (…, period, 36m);  
`releases` (title, platform, region, ts, full history);  
`sentiment_daily_index` / `sentiment_topics` (365d+);  
`forecast_daily` / `forecast_backtest` (12m rolling);  
`alert_definitions` / `alert_events` (12m);  
`sage_recommendations` / `sage_actions_log` (12m);  
`storefront_fees_defaults` / `storefront_fee_overrides` (versioned);  
`price_history` / `iap_price_history` (36m).

**Metric dictionary (selected; all Estimated):**  
DAU; ARPDAU; ARPPU; Conversion; Sentiment index; IAP affordability; MAPE.

**Freshness & quality**: market daily; sentiment hourly-daily; alerts 15m; forecasts daily/weekly. Schema checks; coverage; backfill alerts; backtest logging. Provenance hover shows source & last refresh.

---

## 6) Technical architecture overview
Internal REST per module; no public API v1. Org-scoped data; SSO; RBAC; audit; no PII. Observability on freshness, latency, error budgets; accuracy monitors for forecasting. Feature-flag rollout. Key risks & mitigations: rank→DAU uncertainty (Estimated + provenance); similarity FPs (manual peer controls); fee-policy drift (versioned fee tables); sparse history (conservative features).

---

# Build the Playsage spec as a clean .docx with Glen's approved module names
# and neutral styling (no blue accent boxes). Demo is placed at the end.
# We also resolve the duplicate name "Marketwatch" by naming the releases/collision module "Playsage: Beatmap"
# (per your alt set: Launchscope, Beatmap). If you'd prefer Launchscope, tell me and I'll swap everywhere.

from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_APPROVED_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"  # neutral, readable
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

def KV(doc, pairs):
    return T(doc, ["Key", "Value"], pairs)

def feature_block(doc, f):
    H(doc, f["name"], level=2)
    T(doc, ["A. Summary", "Detail"], [
        ("Purpose", f["purpose"]),
        ("Short description", f["short_desc"]),
        ("Primary use cases", " • " + "\n • ".join(f["use_cases"])),
        ("Estimated value", f["savings"]),
        ("Provenance", "All metrics labeled Estimated with hover details for source, transform, and last refresh"),
    ])
    T(doc, ["B. Design", "Detail"], [
        ("Filters", f["design"]["filters"]),
        ("KPIs displayed", f["design"]["kpis"]),
        ("Views", f["design"]["views"]),
        ("Core interactions & flows", f["design"]["flows"]),
        ("States", f["design"]["states"]),
        ("Error handling & guardrails", f["design"]["errors"]),
        ("Roles & permissions", f["design"]["roles"]),
        ("Acceptance tests", " • " + "\n • ".join(f["accept"])),
        ("Performance SLOs", " • " + "\n • ".join([f"{k}: {v}" for k, v in f["slos"]])),
    ])
    T(doc, ["C. Technical", "Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs & sources", f["tech"]["inputs"]),
        ("Transforms & jobs", f["tech"]["jobs"]),
        ("Storage & models", f["tech"]["storage"]),
        ("Metrics & formulas", f["tech"]["metrics"]),
        ("Algorithms & backtests", f["tech"]["algorithms"]),
        ("Services & endpoints", f["tech"]["services"]),
        ("Security & privacy", f["tech"]["security"]),
        ("Observability", f["tech"]["observability"]),
        ("Feature flags & config", f["tech"]["flags"]),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", f["tech"]["risks"]),
        ("Out of scope (v1)", f["tech"]["out_of_scope"]),
    ])

# --- Begin Document ---

H(doc, "Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec", level=0, center=True)
P(doc, f"Build UTC: {datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M')}")

# Re-run build after transient kernel reset
from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_APPROVED_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

doc = Document()
H(doc, "Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec", level=0, center=True)
P(doc, "Branded modules applied per Glen. Demo placed at end. No tool/file references.")

# Keep doc short to ensure save; detailed content will be appended immediately after save in a second pass.
H(doc, "Branding (locked for this draft)", level=1)
T(doc, ["Module", "Name"], [
    ("Industry overview", "Playsage: Marketwatch"),
    ("Competitive comparisons", "Playsage: Arena"),

from docx import Document
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_APPROVED_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

doc = Document()
H(doc, "Playsage — Product Plan, Design Spec, and Technical Spec", level=0, center=True)

# Generate an updated Playsage spec (.docx) adopting the new module name:
# "Playsage: Launch Control" (replacing the earlier 'Beatmap') for Releases & Collision Risk.
# Neutral styling (no blue accents). Product plan separated from demo. Branded module names applied everywhere.
from docx import Document
from docx.shared import Inches
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.enum.table import WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Spec_Branded_LAUNCH_CONTROL_{TS}.docx"

def H(doc, txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(doc, txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

def T(doc, headers, rows):
    t = doc.add_table(rows=1, cols=len(headers))
    t.style = "Table Grid"  # neutral, readable
    t.alignment = WD_TABLE_ALIGNMENT.LEFT
    for i, h in enumerate(headers):
        t.rows[0].cells[i].text = h
    for row in rows:
        r = t.add_row().cells
        for i, cell in enumerate(row):
            r[i].text = str(cell)
    return t

def KV(doc, pairs):
    return T(doc, ["Key", "Value"], pairs)

def feature_block(doc, f):
    H(doc, f["name"], level=2)
    T(doc, ["A. Summary", "Detail"], [
        ("Purpose", f["purpose"]),
        ("Short description", f["short_desc"]),
        ("Primary use cases", " • " + "\n • ".join(f["use_cases"])),
        ("Estimated value", f["savings"]),
        ("Provenance", "All metrics labeled Estimated with hover details for source, transform, and last refresh"),
    ])
    T(doc, ["B. Design", "Detail"], [
        ("Filters", f["design"]["filters"]),
        ("KPIs displayed", f["design"]["kpis"]),
        ("Views", f["design"]["views"]),
        ("Core interactions & flows", f["design"]["flows"]),
        ("States", f["design"]["states"]),
        ("Error handling & guardrails", f["design"]["errors"]),
        ("Roles & permissions", f["design"]["roles"]),
        ("Acceptance tests", " • " + "\n • ".join(f["accept"])),
        ("Performance SLOs", " • " + "\n • ".join([f"{k}: {v}" for k, v in f["slos"]])),
    ])
    T(doc, ["C. Technical", "Detail"], [
        ("Data inputs & sources", f["tech"]["inputs"]),
        ("Transforms & jobs", f["tech"]["jobs"]),
        ("Storage & models", f["tech"]["storage"]),
        ("Metrics & formulas", f["tech"]["metrics"]),
        ("Algorithms & backtests", f["tech"]["algorithms"]),
        ("Services & endpoints", f["tech"]["services"]),
        ("Security & privacy", f["tech"]["security"]),
        ("Observability", f["tech"]["observability"]),
        ("Feature flags & config", f["tech"]["flags"]),
        ("Dependencies, risks, mitigations", f["tech"]["risks"]),
        ("Out of scope (v1)", f["tech"]["out_of_scope"]),
    ])

# --- Begin Document ---

# Solution path (for your YES/NO)

## A) Formatting overhaul (professional, public-facing)

**Document craft**
- **No meta notes** (no “conflicts,” “assumptions,” or tool references).  
- **Clean Word styles**: Title, Subtitle, Heading 1–3, Body, Caption. No colored boxes.  
- **Numbered outline**: 1., 1.1, 1.2… for traceability.  
- **Auto-generated TOC** (1–3 levels).  
- **Tables only where dense data adds value** (metrics, formulas, endpoints), not as visual layout.  
- **Figure captions** for any diagrams (e.g., “Figure 4 – Launch Control risk score model”).  
- **Footers**: product name, version, date, page X of Y.  
- **House style**: 10.5–11 pt body, 1.15 line spacing, 6/12 pt paragraph spacing, 1.0” margins, left-align; callouts only where essential (warnings/notes).  
- **Appendices** only for reference (metric dictionary, formulas, endpoint lists), not process notes.

**Deliverable split (so each file has a purpose)**
1) **Volume I – Product Plan & PRD** (why, who, goals, scope, success)  
2) **Volume II – Design Spec (UX)** (flows, screens, components, states, a11y)  
3) **Volume III – Technical Spec (Data & Services)** (inputs, jobs, schemas, formulas, models, endpoints, SLOs, observability)  
4) **Volume IV – Demo & Appendix** (demo script, offline plan, metric dictionary, glossary)

(We can also deliver as one master if you prefer; the split mirrors top product orgs’ practice for clarity.)

---

## B) Content overhaul (what “best of breed” includes)

For **each** Playsage module (your approved names: Marketwatch, Arena, Pulse, Foresight, Launch Control, Watchtower, The Sage, Sight, Merchant, Playermap, OrgSight), every section will include:

1) **Problem & Why**  
   - Problem statement (pain & cost), context, “what changed” in the market.  
   - **Value hypothesis** and **measurable outcome** (business and user).

2) **Who**  
   - **Primary persona**, secondary persona, JTBD(s), scenarios.

3) **Goals / Non-goals**  
   - 3–5 outcome goals; explicit non-goals to prevent scope creep.

4) **Use cases** (ranked “must/should/could”)  
   - Each with trigger, entry, success criteria, analytics to track.

5) **KPIs & success metrics**  
   - User-level adoption, time-to-insight, accuracy, ROI impact; targets.

6) **UX specification**  
   - Filters, views, interactions, **states** (loading/empty/partial/offline), **error handling**, accessibility, **voice & tone** microcopy.

7) **Acceptance tests** (user-visible, deterministic).  

8) **Performance SLOs** (P95 latencies, freshness windows, error budgets).  

9) **Data & Algorithms**  
   - Inputs (line-listed sources), transforms & jobs (with cadences), retention, **metrics with explicit formulas**, model choices, **backtests** (MAPE/MAE/RMSE) and guardrails.

10) **Services & Endpoints** (with methods, payloads, auth, limits).  

11) **Security/RBAC & Privacy** (org scoping, audit, PII stance).  

12) **Observability** (what to log, dashboards, alerts & thresholds).  

13) **Feature flags & rollout plan** (dark-launch, staged % rollouts, kill-switches).  

14) **Risks & mitigations** + **Out of scope** (v1).  

15) **Dependencies** (people, data, infra) & **Delivery plan** (M1/M2/M3, entry/exit).  

> You called out “no why / who / goals seeking.” The template above centers on those, then drives to design and implementation with testability.

## C) Sample rewrite (depth bar you should expect everywhere)

### Module: **Playsage: Launch Control** (Releases & Collision Risk)

**1. Problem & Why**  
Studios frequently pick release dates that collide with major beats (AAA launches, expansions, seasonal events), spiking UA costs and cannibalizing attention. The result is lower launch revenue and wasted marketing. Decision-makers lack a **forward-looking, titled-event calendar** that quantifies **collision risk** for their audience, platform, and genre.

**Value hypothesis:** If we forecast and score collision risk with interpretable factors, teams will move dates or marketing cadence to safer windows and improve **first-30-day net revenue** and **organic rank trajectory**.

**2. Who**  
- **Primary:** Publishing Director / Executive Producer (decides dates).  
- **Secondary:** Marketing Lead / UA Lead (spend & beats), Live Ops Manager (events schedule).  
- **JTBD:**  
  - “When I’m choosing a ship window, **help me avoid high-risk collisions** so I can maximize attention and conversion.”  
  - “When competitor beats shift, **alert me with quantified impact** so I can move promo or content.”

**3. Goals & Non-goals**  
- Goals:  
  1) Detect **collisions 2–12 weeks out** with a clear, explainable risk score.  
  2) Reduce **launch collision incidents** by ≥30% for titles using the tool.  
  3) Cut **time-to-decision** (window selection) to <15 minutes from first open.  
- Non-goals (v1): CPI forecasting, sales forecasting; partner embargo calendars.

**4. Must/Should/Could use cases**  
- Must: scan a month, see high-risk weeks with top contributing titles/events; drill to drivers; subscribe to risk changes.  
- Should: export “safe windows” report; filter by platform/region/genre; overlay own internal beats.  
- Could: integrate internal marketing budgets; scenario “if competitor slips by 1 week”.

**5. KPIs**  
- Adoption: weekly active users in Publishing/Marketing ≥ 70% of target cohort.  
- Effect: % of launches moved due to risk insights; **delta revenue vs baseline** for moved launches.  
- Quality: driver coverage ≥ 95%; **false-positive collisions** < 10%.

**6. UX specification**  
- **Filters:** Date window (weeks), platform, region, genre, severity threshold.  
- **Views:**  
  - **Calendar heatmap** (risk score per day/week).  
  - **Drivers list** (titles/events, proximity, scale, audience-overlap).  
  - **Timeline overlays** (your project vs drivers).  
- **Interactions:** click a hot window → drivers → open title sheet → subscribe; “Find safer windows” button proposes 3 alternatives with the delta risk.  
- **States:**  
  - Loading skeletons (<400ms paint).  
  - **Empty:** “No known collisions” with “Add internal event” CTA.  
  - **Partial:** “Console KPI proxies” badge.  
  - Offline: cached calendar + stale banner.  
- **Error handling:** source missing → yellow banner w/ coverage; compute timeout → show last known risk + timestamp.  
- **A11y:** keyboard nav across cells; focus traps; labels; contrast ≥ 4.5:1.  
- **Voice/Tone:** factual, non-alarmist (“High risk due to X and Y; consider shifting ≥ 5 days”).

**7. Acceptance tests**  
- Selecting a 60-day window populates risk cells in ≤ **2.0s P95**.  
- Clicking a high-risk cell opens drivers with **Proximity, Scale, Overlap** values that sum to total risk ±2 tolerance.  
- “Find safer windows” returns ≥ 3 suggestions with Δrisk and drivers removed/added.  
- Subscribing to a change sends an alert within **15 minutes** of recompute.  
- Export produces a single-page brief with date options and rationale.

**8. SLOs**  
- Calendar render P95 ≤ 2.0s; recompute daily (02:00 UTC); alert latency ≤ 15m; error budget < 1%/day.

**9. Data & Algorithms**  
- **Inputs:** public release dates (title/platform/region), content tags & genres, historic rank curves (scale proxy), seasonal event calendars, optional partner calendars (if provided).  
- **Transforms:** daily dedupe/normalization; tag enrichment; platform/region alignment.  
- **Storage:** `releases`, `collision_windows(title, date, platform, region, risk)`, `drivers(title, driver_id, weight, factors)`.  
- **Risk formula (v1, heuristic):**  
  - `Risk = w1*Proximity + w2*Scale + w3*AudienceOverlap + w4*Seasonality`  
  - Proximity = exp(−|Δdays|/λ) · severity; Scale = normalized peak rank of driver in region/platform; Overlap from tag/cluster similarity (Playermap) 0–1; Seasonality from historical demand index. Defaults: w1=0.45, w2=0.30, w3=0.20, w4=0.05; λ=5.  
- **Backtest:** compute historical risk around known launches; correlate with rank/ revenue dips. Report AUC for “collision/no-collision” classification, precision@k for top-risk windows.

**10. Services & Endpoints (internal)**  
- `GET /launch/risk?start&end&platform&region&genre&threshold` → grid of risk scores.  
- `GET /launch/drivers?date&platform&region` → list of drivers with factor breakdown.  
- `POST /launch/subscribe` → rule: date window + filters + threshold.  
- Rate limits: 30 req/min/user; auth: org SSO + RBAC.

**11. Security/RBAC & Privacy**  
- Org-scoped data; no PII; audit for subscriptions/exports; role: Viewer (read), Editor (internal events, exports), Admin (source integrations).

**12. Observability**  
- Metrics: recompute duration, coverage %, driver enrichment success, alert queue depth; alerts on recompute failure, coverage < 90%, render P95 breach.

**13. Flags & rollout**  
- Flags: `risk.weights`, `seasonality.enabled`, `internal_events.enabled`.  
- Rollout: dark-launch (internal), 10% cohort, 50%, 100% with kill switch.

**14. Risks & mitigations**  
- Incomplete calendars → editor input & partner feeds; show coverage badge.  
- Overfitting proximity → backtest tuning; cap daily contributions.  
- False assurance → always present “confidence band” and **drivers**.

**15. Dependencies & delivery plan**  
- Data: releases feed, tag taxonomy, Playermap overlap matrix.  
- Milestones:  
  - M1 calendar heatmap + drivers;  
  - M2 safer windows suggestions + exports;  
  - M3 alerts + partner feeds.

---

### Module: **Playsage: Merchant** (Pricing & IAP)

**1. Problem & Why**  
Pricing mistakes (fees/terms, floors/caps, regional affordability) are expensive and common—especially with changing storefront rules. Teams need a **single simulator** to model fees, taxes, elasticity, and affordability **before** changing prices.

**2. Who**  
- **Primary:** Monetization Lead / Commercial Director.  
- **Secondary:** Live Ops, Finance BP.  
- **JTBD:** “When I tune SKUs, help me forecast **net revenue and payer impact** by region under current policy so I don’t ship bad prices.”

**3. Goals / Non-goals**  
- Goals: single source of fee/policy truth; simulate price moves in < 2s; enforce floors/caps; surface affordability hotspots.  
- Non-goals: experimental ML elasticity per SKU v1.

**4. Use cases**  
- Change a cosmetic bundle from $9.99 → $7.99 in EU; see net and payer deltas under Apple/Google terms.  
- Enforce a price floor for PPV items.  
- Flag countries where affordability < 35.

**5. KPIs**  
- % pricing changes modeled in Merchant before ship (target 100%).  
- Post-change variance vs plan < 10% at 14d.  
- Reduction in pricing reversals ≥ 50%.

**6. UX**  
- Filters: title, region, storefront, item class.  
- Views: **Fee Model** (defaults + overrides + version); **Price Simulator** (A/B vs current); **Affordability Map** (US/UK/EU v1).  
- States/errors: clear floors/caps errors; “needs review” badge if policy stale; offline: cached last model.

**7. Acceptance**  
- Policy toggle changes net in simulator immediately; floors/caps enforced with explicit error; export scenario to CSV/PDF.

**8. SLOs**  
- P95 simulate ≤ 2s; nightly recompute success ≥ 99%; 100% audit of writes.

**9. Data & Algorithms**  
- Inputs: `storefront_fees_defaults`, `storefront_fee_overrides`, `tax_rates`, `refund_rates`, `price_history`, `iap_price_history`.  
- Storage: fees tables (versioned), price histories, `iap_skus`.  
- Formulas (Estimated):  
  - Gross = price × units; Net = Gross − fees − taxes − refunds.  
  - Elasticity: class/band curves E(p) with guardrails; affordability index 0–100 from regional spend power vs price.

**10. Services**  
- `POST /pricing/simulate`; `GET /pricing/fees`; `POST /pricing/override` (role-gated).  
- Audit log on override writes (who/when/what).

**11–15.** As per template (security = role-gated; observability = change logs & recompute latency; flags = Apple-EU/Google-choice; risks = policy drift → versioned tables; delivery M1 simulator, M2 overrides, M3 affordability).

---

## D) What was missing (and now included)

- The **Why/Who/Goals** spine for each feature.  
- **Prioritized use cases** with entry/exit criteria.  
- **Explicit formulas** for metrics (all marked “Estimated”).  
- **Backtests** and accuracy bands for modeled features.  
- **Rollout and feature-flag strategy** (with kill switches).  
- **Instrumentation/observability** plan (metrics, thresholds, alerts).  
- **A11y & UX writing** guidelines.  
- **Clear acceptance tests and SLOs** per module.  
- A **delivery plan** (M1/M2/M3) with dependencies.

# ---------- Helpers to create documents ----------

def apply_base_styles(doc):
    # Set body font to 11pt, headings default
    style = doc.styles['Normal']
    style.font.name = 'Calibri'
    style.font.size = Pt(11)

def add_title(doc, title, subtitle=None):
    h = doc.add_heading(title, 0)
    h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    if subtitle:
        p = doc.add_paragraph(subtitle)
        p.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER

# Volume I – Product Plan & PRD
doc1 = Document()
apply_base_styles(doc1)
add_title(doc1, "Playsage — Volume I: Product Plan & PRD", f"{TS}")

doc1.add_heading("1. Product vision", level=1)
doc1.add_paragraph("Playsage is an applied analytics and advisory suite for game studios and publishers. It unifies industry monitoring, competitive context, sentiment, forecasting with scenarios, release-window risk, pricing & IAP insight, and an advisor that turns signals into next actions.")

doc1.add_heading("2. Personas", level=1)
doc1.add_paragraph("Executives (GM/VP/CEO), Publishing Director/EP, Live Ops Director, Product Manager/Analyst, Economy/Monetization Lead, Marketing/UA Lead, Finance BP.")

doc1.add_heading("3. Supported scope", level=1)
doc1.add_paragraph("Platforms: Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play. Seeded genres: Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy.")

doc1.add_heading("4. Module PRDs", level=1)
for m in modules:
    c = content[m]
    doc1.add_heading(m, level=2)
    doc1.add_paragraph("Problem").bold = True
    doc1.add_paragraph(c["problem"])
    doc1.add_paragraph("Why it matters / Value hypothesis").bold = True
    doc1.add_paragraph(c["value"])
    doc1.add_paragraph("Primary & secondary personas").bold = True
    doc1.add_paragraph(c["personas"])
    doc1.add_paragraph("Jobs-To-Be-Done").bold = True
    for j in c["jtbd"]:
        doc1.add_paragraph(f"• {j}")
    doc1.add_paragraph("Goals").bold = True
    for g in c["goals"]:
        doc1.add_paragraph(f"• {g}")
    if "nongoals" in c:
        doc1.add_paragraph("Non-goals").bold = True
        for g in c["nongoals"]:
            doc1.add_paragraph(f"• {g}")
    doc1.add_paragraph("Use cases (must/should/could)").bold = True
    for u in c["usecases"]:
        doc1.add_paragraph(f"• {u}")
    doc1.add_paragraph("KPIs & Success metrics").bold = True
    for k in c["kpis"]:
        doc1.add_paragraph(f"• {k}")
    doc1.add_paragraph("")

VOL1 = "/mnt/data/Playsage_Volume_I_ProductPlan_PRD.docx"
doc1.save(VOL1)

# Volume II – Design Spec (UX)
doc2 = Document()
apply_base_styles(doc2)
add_title(doc2, "Playsage — Volume II: Design Specification (UX)", f"{TS}")
doc2.add_paragraph("This document specifies the operator experience for each module, including filters, views, interactions, states, error handling, accessibility, microcopy, acceptance tests, and performance SLOs.")

for m in modules:
    c = content[m]
    doc2.add_heading(m, level=1)
    doc2.add_heading("UX blueprint", level=2)
    ux = c["ux"]
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"Filters: {ux['filters']}")
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"Views: {ux['views']}")
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"Core interactions: {ux['interactions']}")
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"States: {ux['states']}")
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"Error handling: {ux['errors']}")
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"Accessibility: {ux['a11y']}")
    doc2.add_paragraph(f"Voice & tone: {ux['microcopy'] if 'microcopy' in ux else 'Factual, concise; avoid hype; surface provenance for Estimated metrics.'}")
    doc2.add_heading("Acceptance tests", level=2)
    for a in c["accept"]:
        doc2.add_paragraph(f"• {a}")
    doc2.add_heading("Performance SLOs", level=2)
    for s in c["slos"]:
        doc2.add_paragraph(f"• {s}")
    doc2.add_paragraph("")

VOL2 = "/mnt/data/Playsage_Volume_II_DesignSpec_UX.docx"
doc2.save(VOL2)

# Volume III – Technical Spec (Data & Services)
doc3 = Document()
apply_base_styles(doc3)
add_title(doc3, "Playsage — Volume III: Technical Specification (Data & Services)", f"{TS}")
doc3.add_paragraph("This document enumerates data inputs, transformations, storage models, explicit metric formulas, algorithms & backtests, services & endpoints, security/RBAC & privacy, observability, feature flags & rollout, risks & mitigations, and delivery plan for each module.")

for m in modules:
    c = content[m]
    t = c["tech"]
    doc3.add_heading(m, level=1)
    doc3.add_heading("Data & processing", level=2)
    doc3.add_paragraph(f"Inputs/Sources: {t['inputs']}")
    doc3.add_paragraph(f"Transforms & Jobs: {t['jobs']}")
    doc3.add_paragraph(f"Storage & Models: {t['storage']}")
    doc3.add_heading("Metrics & formulas (Estimated unless noted)", level=2)
    if isinstance(t["metrics"], list):
        for fmla in t["metrics"]:
            doc3.add_paragraph(f"• {fmla}")
    else:
        doc3.add_paragraph(t["metrics"])
    doc3.add_heading("Algorithms / Backtests", level=2)
    doc3.add_paragraph(t["algos"])
    doc3.add_heading("Services & Endpoints (internal)", level=2)
    for e in t["endpoints"]:
        doc3.add_paragraph(f"• {e}")
    doc3.add_heading("Security / RBAC / Privacy", level=2)
    doc3.add_paragraph(t["security"])
    doc3.add_heading("Observability", level=2)
    doc3.add_paragraph(t["observability"])
    doc3.add_heading("Feature flags / Config", level=2)
    doc3.add_paragraph(t["flags"])
    if "delivery" in t:
        doc3.add_heading("Delivery plan", level=2)
        for d in t["delivery"]:
            doc3.add_paragraph(f"• {d}")
    doc3.add_heading("Risks & Mitigations / Out of scope v1", level=2)
    doc3.add_paragraph(f"Risks: {t['risks']}")
    if "oos" in t:
        doc3.add_paragraph(f"Out of scope: {t['oos']}")
    doc3.add_paragraph("")

VOL3 = "/mnt/data/Playsage_Volume_III_TechSpec_Data_Services.docx"
doc3.save(VOL3)

# Volume IV – Demo & Appendices
doc4 = Document()
apply_base_styles(doc4)
add_title(doc4, "Playsage — Volume IV: Demo & Appendices", f"{TS}")

doc4.add_heading("A. Investor/Executive demo script", level=1)
steps = [

("Drill into Playsage: Marketwatch", "What-Changed cites releases & sentiment; export snapshot."),

("Scan Playsage: Launch Control", "Risk badges explain factors; safer windows suggestions; subscribe."),
("Use Playsage: Merchant", "Toggle fee policy; adjust price; net & affordability update instantly."),
("Ask Playsage: The Sage", "3 recommendations with sources & ranges; export test template."),
]
for i,(act,res) in enumerate(steps,1):
    doc4.add_paragraph(f"{i}) {act} — {res}")

doc4.add_paragraph("Cache all tiles and computed artifacts locally; provide a forced-cache toggle that watermarks exports with build timestamp. Maintain UI parity; sentiment recency may be limited offline. Fallback on compute failure: render last known data with a stale banner.")

gloss = [

]

]
for c in checks:

from docx import Document
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.shared import Pt
from datetime import datetime

def apply_base_styles(doc):
    style = doc.styles['Normal']
    style.font.name = 'Calibri'
    style.font.size = Pt(11)

def add_title(doc, title, subtitle=None):
    h = doc.add_heading(title, 0)
    h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    if subtitle:
        p = doc.add_paragraph(subtitle)
        p.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
