# Playsage — Volume I: Product Plan & PRD

## 1. Product vision
Playsage turns fragmented industry signals into decisions for studios and publishers. It unifies: market health, competitive context, sentiment intelligence, forecasting with scenarios, release-window risk, pricing & IAP insight, and an embedded advisor that converts signals into next-best actions.

## 2. Personas
Executives (CEO/GM/VP), Publishing Director/EP, Live Ops Director, Product Manager/Analyst, Monetization Lead/Economy Designer, Marketing/UA Lead, Finance BP.

## 3. Scope
**Platforms**: Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play.  
**Seeded genres**: Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy.  
**Investor-demo success**: P95 tile latency ≤ 3s; visible “Estimated” provenance; forecast backtests shown; offline parity (forced cache); board-ready exports.

---

## 4. Module PRDs

### 4.1 Playsage: Marketwatch
**Problem** — Leaders bounce between screenshots and stitched dashboards; there’s no single, defensible view of market health by platform/region/genre.  
**Why/Value** — A single narrative (“What changed and why”) reduces ad-hoc analysis by 6–10 hours/week and aligns portfolio bets.

**Personas** — Primary: Executive (GM/VP); Secondary: Strategy/BD, Product Director.  
**JTBD** — (1) “Show me growth, share, and movers so I can steer portfolio bets.” (2) “Produce a defensible snapshot for the board in minutes.”

**Goals** — Single-page narrative; evidence-backed “What Changed”; time-to-insight < 5 min.  
**Non-goals** — Paid media modeling; console net revenue modeling (v1).

**Must/Should/Could Use Cases**  
- Must: scan market momentum; drill movers with drivers; export a brief.  
- Should: save portfolio views; compare current vs prior quarter.  
- Could: annotate and share a snapshot link.

**KPIs** — Exec WAU ≥ 70% of target; export in < 3 min; coverage ≥ 95% of supported scope.

---

### 4.2 Playsage: Arena
**Problem** — Peer sets are inconsistent; teams can’t quickly explain rank shifts with evidence.  
**Value** — Defensible head-to-head with releases, cadence, sentiment, and monetization signatures; saves 4–6 hours per comparison.

**Personas** — Primary: Product Director; Secondary: Analyst, UA Lead.  
**JTBD** — Compare to the right peers; explain rank shifts with evidence.

**Goals** — Accurate, editable peer sets; overlays explain changes; export H2H in < 3 min.  
**Non-goals** — Player-level cohort analysis (v1).

**Use Cases** — Create/save peer sets; overlay releases/pricing; export H2H with evidence.  
**KPIs** — Editor adoption ≥ 60% of PM/Analyst cohort; ≥ 80% exports include ≥ 2 evidence artifacts; P95 timeline ≤ 2.5s.

---

### 4.3 Playsage: Pulse
**Problem** — Sentiment is fragmented; teams see performance move before they see why.  
**Value** — Daily sentiment index & topic map; earlier detection of issues (5–8 analyst hours/week saved).

**Personas** — Primary: Community/Live Ops Manager; Secondary: PM, Support.  
**JTBD** — Track player mood; get alerted on new negative themes before KPIs drop.

**Goals** — Reliable index (0–100); actionable topics with exemplars; alerts within 15m.  
**Non-goals** — Private community data (v1).

**Use Cases** — Scan delta; open topics & exemplars; subscribe to spikes; export weekly brief.  
**KPIs** — P95 tile ≤ 2s; alert ≤ 15m; topic precision (spot-check) ≥ 80%.

---

### 4.4 Playsage: Foresight
**Problem** — Forecasts are black-box or absent; impact of content, price, and IAP is guesswork.  
**Value** — Explainable 90-day forecasts with backtests and scenario controls; +5–15% promo ROI.

**Personas** — Primary: Live Ops Director; Secondary: PM, Finance BP.  
**JTBD** — Project DAU/revenue with bands; quantify expected lift of changes.

**Goals** — Transparent backtests; editable levers; download scenario plan.  
**Non-goals** — Player-level uplift attribution (v1).

**Use Cases** — Baseline with bands; scenario compare; export plan; degrade-accuracy alerts.  
**KPIs** — MAPE displayed by horizon; scenario adoption ≥ 60% of Live Ops titles/month.

---

### 4.5 Playsage: Launch Control
**Problem** — Launches and events collide with major beats; attention cannibalized, UA costs spike.  
**Value** — Quantified collision risk & safer windows; ≥ 30% fewer collisions.

**Personas** — Primary: Publishing Director/EP; Secondary: Marketing Lead, Live Ops.  
**JTBD** — Pick safer release windows; adjust marketing when competitors shift.

**Goals** — Explainable risk score with drivers; one-click safer window suggestions.  
**Non-goals** — CPI forecasting (v1).

**Use Cases** — Scan 60-day heatmap; drill drivers; subscribe risk changes; export safer options.  
**KPIs** — Calendar P95 ≤ 2.0s; alert ≤ 15m; % launches moved due to insight; Δrevenue vs baseline.

---

### 4.6 Playsage: Watchtower
**Problem** — Teams get notified too late or are spammed by noisy rules.  
**Value** — Right-sized, deduped alerts & digests across KPIs, sentiment, and launch risk; saves 1–3 hours/day.

**Personas** — Primary: PM/Analyst; Secondary: Live Ops, Exec.  
**JTBD** — Catch swings early; get a weekly brief without babysitting dashboards.

**Goals** — Simple rule builder; multi-channel delivery; low false-positive rate.  
**Non-goals** — Advanced anomaly ML (v1).

**Use Cases** — Create KPI threshold rule with backfill test; subscribe to weekly digest; cooldown noisy rules.  
**KPIs** — Delivery ≥ 99%; FPR < 10%; UI feed P95 ≤ 1.5s.

---

### 4.7 Playsage: The Sage
**Problem** — Teams have data but lack guidance; plans are inconsistent and slow.  
**Value** — Embedded advisor that turns signals into next-best actions with ranges; plan two sprints in minutes.

**Personas** — Primary: Live Ops Director; Secondary: PM, CRM.  
**JTBD** — Prioritized actions with expected impact; export test templates.

**Goals** — ≥ 3 recommendations/title; evidence cited; ranges with confidence.  
**Non-goals** — ASO fixes, bug triage prompts.

**Use Cases** — Ask for 2-sprint plan; export A/B plan (metrics & stop rules); track acceptance & outcomes.  
**KPIs** — Coverage ≥ 3 recs/title; P95 latency ≤ 2s; acceptance rate tracked.

---

### 4.8 Playsage: Sight
**Problem** — Execs need a live, presenter-ready view; teams waste time reformatting.  
**Value** — Six-tile default, presenter mode, one-click export; consistent narrative.

**Personas** — Primary: GM/VP/CEO; Secondary: PM leads.  
**JTBD** — Present live; export the board page.

**Goals** — Default six tiles; presenter mode; branded export.  
**Non-goals** — Public share links (v1).

**Use Cases** — Load default; reorder & save org preset; present; export; reset to default.  
**KPIs** — Load P95 ≤ 2s; export ≤ 3s; preset adoption ≥ 70%.

---

### 4.9 Playsage: Merchant
**Problem** — Pricing changes ship without seeing net impact under evolving policies; affordability opaque.  
**Value** — Simulate fees/taxes/elasticity/affordability with guardrails & overrides.

**Personas** — Primary: Monetization Lead/Commercial Director; Secondary: Live Ops, Finance.  
**JTBD** — Model net revenue before changes; enforce floors/caps; see affordability hotspots.

**Goals** — Single policy truth; simulate < 2s; enforce guardrails.  
**Non-goals** — Country-level affordability (v1).

**Use Cases** — Toggle Apple-EU/Google-choice; simulate SKU; save per-title override; export price plan.  
**KPIs** — 100% price changes simulated pre-ship; variance vs plan at 14d < 10%; pricing reversals ↓ 50%.

---

### 4.10 Playsage: Playermap
**Problem** — Overlap guessed from anecdotes; lookalikes missed.  
**Value** — Interpretable clusters & overlaps drive UA, bundles, positioning.

**Personas** — Primary: UA Lead/PMM; Secondary: BizDev, PM.  
**JTBD** — Find lookalikes; validate features against cluster preferences.

**Goals** — Stable clusters with interpretable labels; export lookalikes.  
**Non-goals** — Player-level graph (v1).

**Use Cases** — View cluster card; export lookalikes; track cluster movement MoM.  
**KPIs** — P95 ≤ 2s; stability ≥ 30d; ≥ 5 lookalikes/flagship.

---

### 4.11 Playsage: OrgSight
**Problem** — Org cadence and health tracked in spreadsheets; no link to outcomes.  
**Value** — Light diagnostics and action plans aligned to advisory.

**Personas** — Primary: CEO/Studio Head; Secondary: Production Director.  
**JTBD** — Understand bottlenecks; align exec cadence to product milestones.

**Goals** — Simple indices; no personal data; actionable exports.  
**Non-goals** — Employee-level analytics.

**Use Cases** — Run diagnostic; attach actions/owners; export offsite pack.  
**KPIs** — Pack export < 3s; leadership adoption ≥ 70%.

---

# Playsage — Volume II: Design Specification (UX)

_For each module: filters, views, interactions, states, error handling, accessibility, microcopy, acceptance tests, SLOs._

## Marketwatch (UX)
- **Filters**: Date, Platform, Region, Genre, Title set  
- **Views**: Overview KPIs; trends with prior overlay; “What Changed” narrative; drill-downs  
- **Interactions**: Click delta → drivers (releases, sentiment, pricing) with timestamps; save/export snapshot; save view  
- **States**: Skeletons; guided empty; partial (low-history) badge; offline cached snapshot  
- **Errors**: Stale banner; fallback to last known snapshot  
- **A11y**: Keyboard navigation; readable tooltips; visible focus; contrast ≥ 4.5:1  
- **Voice & tone**: Factual, sourced; modeled numbers labeled **Estimated** with provenance

**Acceptance tests** — overview paints ≤ 2.5s P95; “What Changed” lists ≥ 3 drivers; export is single-page, brand-compliant.  
**SLOs** — P95 ≤ 3s; daily freshness; error budget < 1%/day.

---

## Arena (UX)
- **Filters**: Title, Peer set, Platform, Region, Version pin, Date range  
- **Views**: Peer grid; head-to-head timeline; monetization signature badges  
- **Interactions**: Add/remove peers; pin versions; toggle overlays; export with evidence links  
- **States**: No-peers prompt; partial data badges; skeletons  
- **Errors**: Outlier annotations; console KPI placeholders  
- **A11y**: ARIA labels for toggles; keyboard timelines

**Acceptance** — peer set created & saved < 60s; timeline renders ≤ 2.5s; export includes driver links.  
**SLOs** — P95 ≤ 2.5s; daily freshness; backfill < 2h.

---

## Pulse (UX)
- **Filters**: Title, Platform, Region, Source, Window  
- **Views**: Index line; topic tiles; exemplar drawer  
- **Interactions**: Delta → topic → exemplars; subscribe to spikes  
- **States**: Guided empty; low-history badge; skeletons  
- **Errors**: Coverage banners; cached fallback  
- **A11y**: Keyboard readable; semantic topic labels

**Acceptance** — delta cards show counts & window; alert ≤ 15m; export has definition tooltips.  
**SLOs** — processing ≤ 1h; P95 ≤ 2s; alert ≤ 15m.

---

## Foresight (UX)
- **Filters**: Title, Platform, Region, Horizon, Confidence, Scenario set  
- **Views**: Forecast with bands; drivers & weights; compare table  
- **Interactions**: Adjust levers; save scenario; export plan  
- **States**: Low-history warning; offline baseline  
- **Errors**: Lever stacking caps; provenance badges  
- **A11y**: Keyboard for sliders; accessible data tables

**Acceptance** — backtest ribbon shows MAPE+window; scenario export includes levers & bands; render ≤ 3s.  
**SLOs** — P95 ≤ 3s; backtest coverage 100% demo titles; retrain daily/weekly.

---

## Launch Control (UX)
- **Filters**: Date window, Platform, Region, Genre, Severity  
- **Views**: Calendar heatmap; drivers list; timeline overlays  
- **Interactions**: Click cell → drivers; “Find safer windows” → ≥ 3 suggestions with Δrisk  
- **States**: Empty with “Add internal event” CTA; partial proxies; offline cached  
- **Errors**: Coverage badge; fallback to last compute  
- **A11y**: Keyboard cell nav; driver list accessible

**Acceptance** — drivers sum to risk ±2; suggestions include Δrisk and key drivers; alert ≤ 15m.  
**SLOs** — P95 ≤ 2s; daily recompute; alert ≤ 15m.

---

## Watchtower (UX)
- **Rule builder**; alert feed; digest scheduler; multi-channel delivery  
- **Acceptance** — create-test-save in < 60s; delivery logs show success/retry; digest readable A4/Letter  
**SLOs** — 15m streaming cadence; delivery ≥ 99%; feed P95 ≤ 1.5s.

---

## The Sage (UX)
- **Views**: Recommendations with evidence & ranges; acceptance log; export test template  
- **Acceptance** — each rec shows sources & “Estimated”; export includes steps/metrics/stop rules; latency ≤ 2s  
**SLOs** — P95 ≤ 2s; export ≤ 2s; coverage ≥ 3 recs/title.

---

## Sight (UX)
- **Views**: Six-tile grid; presenter mode; export PDF/PNG/PPT; save org preset  
- **Acceptance** — default tiles on first load; presenter improves readability; export brand-compliant  
**SLOs** — load P95 ≤ 2s; export ≤ 3s.

---

## Merchant (UX)
- **Views**: Fee Model (defaults/overrides/version); Price Simulator; Affordability Map (US/UK/EU v1)  
- **Acceptance** — policy toggle updates net instantly; floors/caps enforced with clear errors; affordability visible  
**SLOs** — simulate P95 ≤ 2s; nightly recompute ≥ 99%; audit 100%.

---

## Playermap (UX)
- **Views**: Cluster cards; overlap matrix; movement over time  
- **Acceptance** — card lists name/size/growth/top titles/tags; overlap exports CSV/PNG; P95 ≤ 2s  
**SLOs** — P95 ≤ 2s; stability ≥ 30d.

---

## OrgSight (UX)
- **Views**: Diagnostic tiles; action plans with owners/dates; export PDF  
- **Acceptance** — no personal data; index tooltips; export ≤ 3s  
**SLOs** — monthly refresh; export ≤ 3s.

---

# Playsage — Volume III: Technical Specification (Data & Services)

_For each module: inputs, jobs, storage, formulas, algorithms & backtests, endpoints, security/RBAC & privacy, observability, feature flags, risks & mitigations, delivery._

## Marketwatch (Tech)
- **Inputs**: store ranks/tags; aggregated reviews; sentiment index; releases  
- **Jobs**: hourly ingests (where available); daily normalization; genre assignment; “What Changed” diffs  
- **Storage**: `kpi_daily(title,platform,region,date)`; `kpi_periodic(...,period)`; `releases(...,ts)`; `sentiment_daily_index(...,date)`  
- **Formulas (Estimated)**: market share = DAU proxy ÷ platform total; growth = (curr−prior)/prior; mover score = z-score(w/w delta)  
- **Algorithms**: windowed diffs; z-scores; narrative templating  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /tiles/market/overview`, `GET /tiles/market/diffs`, `POST /exports/market/snapshot`  
- **Security**: org scope; SSO; RBAC; no PII; export audit  
- **Observability**: freshness, P95 tile latency, diff job success  
- **Flags**: anomaly thresholds; mover toggle  
- **Risks**: rank→DAU uncertainty → **Estimated** with provenance  
- **Delivery**: M1 overviews+diffs; M2 saved views/export; M3 portfolio presets

---

## Arena (Tech)
- **Inputs**: `kpi_daily`; `releases`; `sentiment_daily_index`; `monetization_signatures`; `price_history`  
- **Jobs**: daily peer refresh; release alignment; version pin  
- **Storage**: `compare_snapshots(id,org,title,peer_ids,ts)`; `monetization_signatures(title,signature)`  
- **Formulas**: rank Δ vs peers = rank_pct(title)−mean(rank_pct(peers)); cadence variance = std(days_between_updates)  
- **Algo**: tag/curve similarity (auto) + manual override  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /compare/peers`, `GET /compare/h2h`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: org/title scoping; masking; audit; enable signature overlays; similarity FP mitigated by manual controls

---

## Pulse (Tech)
- **Inputs**: store reviews; public social; language normalizer; spam/bot filters  
- **Jobs**: daily collection/normalization; topic detection & dedupe  
- **Storage**: `sentiment_daily_index`; `sentiment_topics(title,platform,region,date,topic,volume,polarity)`  
- **Formulas**: index = normalized polarity scaled 0–100; spike threshold = EWMA(μ)+k·σ  
- **Algo**: polarity classifier; topic modeling (NMF/LDA) + smoothing; spam heuristics  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /sentiment/index`, `GET /sentiment/topics`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: public data only; no PII; false-positive tracking; smoothing factor; sarcasm/drift mitigated via spot-checks

---

## Foresight (Tech)
- **Inputs**: `kpi_daily`; `releases`; `price_history`; `monetization_signatures`; `sentiment_daily_index`  
- **Jobs**: rolling backtests; daily/weekly retrains; attribution builds  
- **Storage**: `forecast_daily`; `forecast_backtest`; `forecast_attribution`  
- **Formulas**: MAPE = mean(|y−ŷ|/y); RMSE = sqrt(mean((y−ŷ)^2))  
- **Algo**: GBM/Prophet + calendar & release features; attribution via SHAP/permutation  
- **Endpoints**: `POST /forecast/run`, `POST /forecast/scenario`, `GET /forecast/backtest`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: org-scoped models; versioned; accuracy/latency monitors; detrending toggle; sparse history mitigated by conservative features

---

## Launch Control (Tech)
- **Inputs**: releases; content_tags; historic rank curves; seasonal events; optional partner calendars  
- **Jobs**: daily recompute; driver enrichment; suggestion generation  
- **Storage**: `collision_windows(title,date,platform,region,risk)`; `drivers(title,driver_id,weight,factors)`; `suggestions(date,alt_window,delta_risk)`  
- **Formula**: Risk = 0.45·Proximity + 0.30·Scale + 0.20·Overlap + 0.05·Seasonality; Proximity = exp(−|Δdays|/5)·severity  
- **Algo**: heuristic with tunable weights; backtests vs historical dips; precision@k on top-risk windows  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /launch/risk`, `GET /launch/drivers`, `POST /launch/subscribe`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: org scope; no PII; coverage/queue monitors; `risk.weights`, `seasonality.enabled`, `internal_events.enabled`; incomplete calendars mitigated via editor input & partner feeds

---

## Watchtower (Tech)
- **Inputs**: tile metrics; sentiment/launch signals  
- **Jobs**: streaming checks every 15m; daily digests  
- **Storage**: `alert_definitions`; `alert_events`  
- **Metrics**: time-to-notify; false-positive rate; delivery success  
- **Algo**: threshold rules v1; anomaly bands later  
- **Endpoints**: `/alerts/*` (internal)  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: per-user scopes; audit; GDPR; queue depth & retries; anomaly mode toggles; noisy rules mitigated by cooldown/dedupe

---

## The Sage (Tech)
- **Inputs**: public signals + optional uploads; competitor pricing/IAP; cadence; sentiment  
- **Jobs**: periodic refresh; on-demand generation  
- **Storage**: `sage_recommendations`; `sage_actions_log`  
- **Metrics**: confidence band width; acceptance rate  
- **Algo**: retrieval + prompt templates; rules/priors for lift ranges  
- **Endpoints**: `POST /sage/ask`, `GET /sage/recommend`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: strict scoping; audit; no PII; acceptance telemetry; action-type toggles; lift caps; overreach mitigated via explicit out-of-scope

---

## Sight (Tech)
- **Inputs**: underlying tiles; layout metadata  
- **Storage**: `dashboard_layouts`; `presets`  
- **Endpoints**: `/dashboard/*` (internal)  
- **Obs/Flags/Risks**: layout errors; export latency; presenter toggle; reset-to-default mitigates over-customization

---

## Merchant (Tech)
- **Inputs**: `fees_defaults/overrides`; `tax_rates`; `refund_rates`; `price_history`; `iap_price_history`  
- **Jobs**: nightly recompute net & affordability  
- **Storage**: fees tables (versioned); `price_history`; `iap_skus`; `iap_price_history`  
- **Formulas**: Gross = price×units; Net = Gross − fees − taxes − refunds; Affordability index 0–100 vs regional spend power; elasticity by class/band  
- **Endpoints**: `POST /pricing/simulate`, `GET /pricing/fees`, `POST /pricing/override`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: role-gated writes; audit trail; change logs; recompute latency; Apple-EU & Google-choice toggles; policy drift mitigated by versioned fees

---

## Playermap (Tech)
- **Inputs**: store signals; rank curves; tags; review vectors; optional overlap feeds  
- **Jobs**: daily graph updates; weekly stability checks  
- **Storage**: `cluster_nodes`; `cluster_edges`; `overlap_matrices`  
- **Metrics**: Overlap% = shared_audience / min(audA,audB); silhouette score  
- **Algo**: multi-view similarity; density clustering; interpretable labels  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /affinity/graph`, `GET /clusters/cards`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: no PII; drift alerts; cluster size limits; smoothing; overfitting mitigated by multi-source inputs

---

## OrgSight (Tech)
- **Inputs**: Playsage aggregate indices; optional survey inputs (non-PII)  
- **Jobs**: monthly refresh; on-demand runs  
- **Storage**: `org_diagnostics(org,team,date,indexes,notes)`; `org_actions(id,owner,due,status)`  
- **Algo**: heuristic scoring; indices normalized 0–100  
- **Endpoints**: `GET /org/diagnostics`, `POST /org/actions`  
- **Security/Obs/Flags/Risks**: org scope; no personal data; compliance logs; enable per org; interpretation risk mitigated via guidance

---

# Playsage — Volume IV: Demo & Appendices

## A. Investor/Executive demo script
1) **Sight** — Six tiles load ≤ 2s; “Estimated” provenance visible.  
2) **Marketwatch** — “What Changed” cites releases & sentiment; export snapshot.  
3) **Arena** — Add peers; timeline ≤ 2.5s; overlays; evidence links.  
4) **Pulse** — Subscribe spike alert; test event delivered ≤ 15m.  
5) **Foresight** — Baseline vs scenario; backtest ribbon; export plan with bands.  
6) **Launch Control** — Risk badges explain factors; safer window suggestions; subscribe.  
7) **Merchant** — Toggle policy; adjust price; net & affordability update.  
8) **The Sage** — 3 recs with sources & ranges; export test template.

## B. Offline demo plan
Cache tiles and computed artifacts; forced-cache toggle watermarks exports with build timestamp. UI parity; sentiment recency may be limited offline. On compute failure, render last known with stale banner.

## C. Metric dictionary (selected)
- DAU (Estimated): rank→DAU mapping per platform with calibration  
- ARPDAU (Estimated): net revenue ÷ DAU  
- ARPPU (Estimated): net revenue ÷ payers  
- Conversion (Estimated): payers ÷ DAU  
- Sentiment index: normalized polarity 0–100 with smoothing  
- IAP affordability: scaled 0–100 vs regional benchmarks  
- MAPE; RMSE (forecast accuracy)

## D. Endpoint index (by module)
- Marketwatch — `GET /tiles/market/overview`, `GET /tiles/market/diffs`, `POST /exports/market/snapshot`  
- Arena — `GET /compare/peers`, `GET /compare/h2h`  
- Pulse — `GET /sentiment/index`, `GET /sentiment/topics`  
- Foresight — `POST /forecast/run`, `POST /forecast/scenario`, `GET /forecast/backtest`  
- Launch Control — `GET /launch/risk`, `GET /launch/drivers`, `POST /launch/subscribe`  
- Watchtower — `/alerts/*` (internal)  
- The Sage — `POST /sage/ask`, `GET /sage/recommend`  
- Sight — `/dashboard/*` (internal)  
- Merchant — `POST /pricing/simulate`, `GET /pricing/fees`, `POST /pricing/override`  
- Playermap — `GET /affinity/graph`, `GET /clusters/cards`  
- OrgSight — `GET /org/diagnostics`, `POST /org/actions`

## E. Glossary
TAM/SAM; Collision risk; Monetization signature; Provenance; Confidence band; Stability window.

## F. Compliance checklist
- All modeled metrics labeled **Estimated** with provenance  
- No PII; org scoping enforced; SSO + RBAC  
- Audit logs on exports, overrides, subscriptions  
- P95/SLOs defined per module; alert on breach  
- Accessibility: WCAG 2.1 AA goals documented

---

- Added **acceptance tests** and **SLOs** per module.  
- Included explicit **formulas** and **algorithms/backtests** where modeling is involved.  
- Defined **endpoints**, **security**, **observability**, **feature flags**, **rollout**.  
- Split deliverables into **four volumes** following best-of-breed product org practice.

# Helpers
def apply_base_styles(doc):
    style = doc.styles['Normal']
    style.font.name = 'Calibri'
    style.font.size = Pt(11)

    h = doc.add_heading(title, 0)
    h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    if subtitle:
        p = doc.add_paragraph(subtitle

# Build the document
doc = Document()
# Set base styles
style = doc.styles['Normal']
style.font.name = 'Calibri'
style.font.size = Pt(11)

# Title
title = doc.add_heading("Playsage — Volume I: Product Plan & PRD", 0)
title.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
subtitle = doc.add_paragraph(f"{TS}")
subtitle.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER

# Vision
doc.add_heading("1. Product vision", level=1)
doc.add_paragraph("Playsage turns fragmented industry signals into decisions for studios and publishers. It unifies: market health, competitive context, sentiment intelligence, forecasting with scenarios, release-window risk, pricing & IAP insight, audience mapping, and an embedded advisor that converts signals into next-best actions.")

# Personas
doc.add_heading("2. Personas", level=1)
doc.add_paragraph("Executives (CEO/GM/VP), Publishing Director/EP, Live Ops Director, Product Manager/Analyst, Monetization Lead/Economy Designer, Marketing/UA Lead, Finance BP.")

# Scope
doc.add_heading("3. Scope", level=1)
doc.add_paragraph("Platforms: Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play.")
doc.add_paragraph("Seeded genres: Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy.")
doc.add_paragraph("Investor-demo success: P95 tile latency ≤ 3s; visible 'Estimated' provenance; forecast backtests shown; offline parity via forced cache; board-ready exports.")

# Product principles
doc.add_heading("4. Product principles", level=1)
principles = [
"Decisions, not dashboards: every screen answers a question and proposes an action.",
"Explainability: 'Estimated' labels with provenance are first-class UI.",
"Fast by default: P95 latencies and freshness windows are user-facing commitments.",
"Accessibility: WCAG 2.1 AA targets; keyboard-first workflows in data-dense views.",
"Export quality: every tile supports board-ready exports without reformatting."
]
for p in principles:
    doc.add_paragraph(f"• {p}")

# Module PRDs
doc.add_heading("5. Module PRDs", level=1)
for m in modules:
    cx = C[m]
    doc.add_heading(m, level=2)
    doc.add_heading("Problem", level=3)
    doc.add_paragraph(cx["problem"])
    doc.add_heading("Why it matters / Value", level=3)
    doc.add_paragraph(cx["value"])
    doc.add_heading("Primary & secondary personas", level=3)
    doc.add_paragraph(cx["personas"])
    doc.add_heading("Jobs-To-Be-Done", level=3)
    for j in cx["jtbd"]:
        doc.add_paragraph(f"• {j}")
    doc.add_heading("Goals", level=3)
    for g in cx["goals"]:
        doc.add_paragraph(f"• {g}")
    if cx["nongoals"]:
        doc.add_heading("Non-goals", level=3)
        for ng in cx["nongoals"]:
            doc.add_paragraph(f"• {ng}")
    doc.add_heading("Use cases (must/should/could)", level=3)
    for u in cx["usecases"]:
        doc.add_paragraph(f"• {u}")
    doc.add_heading("Success metrics & targets", level=3)
    for k in cx["kpis"]:
        doc.add_paragraph(f"• {k}")
    doc.add_paragraph("")

# Cross-cutting success metrics
doc.add_heading("6. Cross-cutting success metrics", level=1)
cross = [
"Weekly active decision-makers (Exec/Publishing/Live Ops) ≥ 70% of target cohort by month 3.",
"Median time-to-insight < 5 minutes for Marketwatch/Arena/Launch Control.",
"Forecast accuracy (MAPE) tracked and visible in-app by horizon; degradation alerting enabled.",
"Export usage ≥ 50% of exec sessions; exports meet brand guidelines without editing."
]
for item in cross:
    doc.add_paragraph(f"• {item}")

# Release plan
doc.add_heading("7. Release plan & milestones", level=1)
milestones = [
"M1 (Foundations): Marketwatch, Arena (baseline), Sight defaults; exports; provenance labels.",
"M2 (Signal depth): Pulse, Launch Control, Watchtower; alerting; saved views/presets.",
"M3 (Decide & simulate): Foresight (scenarios), Merchant, Playermap, The Sage; org rollout."
]
for m in milestones:
    doc.add_paragraph(f"• {m}")

# Risks & mitigations
doc.add_heading("8. Risks & mitigations", level=1)
risks = [
"Rank→DAU mapping uncertainty — Mitigation: label Estimated, show provenance, use conservative calibration.",
"Similarity false-positives (Arena/Playermap) — Mitigation: manual peer controls; explain-why cards.",
"Incomplete release calendars (Launch Control) — Mitigation: editor inputs; partner feeds; coverage badges.",
"Policy drift (Merchant) — Mitigation: versioned fee tables; needs-review badges."
]
for r in risks:
    doc.add_paragraph(f"• {r}")

# Packaging & pricing (high level)
doc.add_heading("9. Packaging & pricing (high level)", level=1)
doc.add_paragraph("Packaging to be finalized with GTM: Core (Marketwatch, Arena, Sight), Growth (adds Pulse, Launch Control, Watchtower), Pro (adds Foresight, Merchant, Playermap, The Sage), with optional OrgSight add-on. Pricing TBD per seat + data tier.")

# Playsage — Volume I: Product Plan & PRD

## 1. Product vision
Playsage turns fragmented industry signals into decisions for studios and publishers. The suite unifies:
- Industry health and “what changed” (Marketwatch)
- Competitive context and peer comparisons (Arena)
- Sentiment and topic intelligence (Pulse)
- Forecasts with scenarios and backtests (Foresight)
- Release-window risk and safer dates (Launch Control)
- Alerts and executive digests (Watchtower)
- An embedded advisor with expected ranges (The Sage)
- Executive dashboard presets (Sight)
- Pricing/IAP simulator and fees (Merchant)
- Audience overlaps and lookalikes (Playermap)
- Optional leadership diagnostics (OrgSight)

Core principles: decisions over dashboards; transparent “Estimated” labels with provenance; fast-by-default (P95 latencies & freshness are first-class); WCAG 2.1 AA; board-ready exports.

## 2. Personas (primary → secondary)
- Publishing Director / Executive Producer → Marketing Lead, Live Ops Manager
- Live Ops Director → PM/Analyst, Finance BP
- GM/VP/CEO → PM leads
- Product Manager / Analyst → UA Lead, PMM
- Monetization/Economy Lead → Finance BP
- CEO/Studio Head (OrgSight add-on)

## 3. Scope
Platforms: Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play  
Seeded genres: Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy  
Investor-demo success: P95 tile ≤ 3s; “Estimated” provenance visible; forecast backtests shown; offline forced-cache parity; board-ready export.

---

## 4. Module PRDs (why/who/goals/use cases/KPIs)

### 4.1 Playsage: Marketwatch
**Problem**  
Leaders lack one defensible view of market health by platform/region/genre; stitched screenshots slow decisions and create disagreement.

**Why / Value**  
A single, evidence-backed narrative (“what changed and why”) cuts 6–10 analyst hours/week and aligns portfolio bets.

**Who**  
Primary: Executive (GM/VP)  
Secondary: Strategy/BD, Product Director

**Goals**  
- Single-page market narrative with defensible numbers  
- Show “what changed” with cited drivers (releases, sentiment, pricing)  
- Time-to-insight < 5 minutes from open

**Non-goals**  
Paid media modeling; console net revenue modeling (v1)

**Use cases (must/should/could)**  
- **Must — Weekly momentum scan**  
  Trigger: Monday exec review → Entry: select platform/region/genre → Steps: view movers, open “why,” export brief → Success: brief exported in <3 minutes with three cited drivers  
- **Must — Driver drill**  
  Trigger: board ask “why did X rise?” → Steps: open mover, view releases/sentiment/pricing deltas → Success: answer with evidence in <5 minutes  
- **Should — Portfolio view**  
  Steps: save title set, schedule weekly brief → Success: portfolio preset adopted by execs  
- **Could — Annotated snapshot**  
  Success: snapshot with annotations shared to leadership

**KPIs & targets**  
Exec WAU ≥ 70% of target; export < 3 minutes; coverage ≥ 95% of supported scope

---

### 4.2 Playsage: Arena
**Problem**  
Peer sets are inconsistent; teams can’t explain rank shifts with evidence.

**Value**  
Defensible head-to-head with releases, cadence, sentiment, monetization signatures; saves 4–6 hours per comparison.

**Who**  
Primary: Product Director  
Secondary: Analyst, UA Lead

**Goals**  
Accurate, editable peer sets; overlays explain change; export H2H in < 3 minutes

**Non-goals**  
Player-level cohorts (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Build & save peer set**  
  Trigger: new roadmap review → Steps: auto-suggest peers, edit, save org-wide → Success: peer set reused across team  
- **Must — Explain rank swing**  
  Trigger: week-over-week drop → Steps: overlay releases/pricing/sentiment → Success: 2+ evidence items attached to export  
- **Should — Version pin**  
  Trigger: major update → Steps: pin version; compare before/after → Success: clear delta narrative  
- **Could — Signature comparison**  
  Success: signature badges highlight monetization model differences

**KPIs**  
Editor adoption ≥ 60%; ≥ 80% exports include ≥ 2 evidence artifacts; P95 timeline ≤ 2.5s

---

### 4.3 Playsage: Pulse
**Problem**  
Sentiment is fragmented; teams see KPIs move before they see why.

**Value**  
Daily sentiment index & topic map; earlier detection of issues; 5–8 hours/week saved.

**Who**  
Primary: Community/Live Ops  
Secondary: PM, Support

**Goals**  
Reliable index (0–100); actionable topics; spike alerts ≤ 15m

**Non-goals**  
Private community data (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Delta + topics** → Success: topic exemplars explain delta within 3 clicks  
- **Must — Spike alert** → Success: alert fires ≤ 15m after threshold breach  
- **Should — Weekly brief export** → Success: brief consumed by execs  
- **Could — Topic watchlist** → Success: tracked topics with trend indicators

**KPIs**  
Tile P95 ≤ 2s; alert ≤ 15m; spot-check topic precision ≥ 80%

---

### 4.4 Playsage: Foresight
**Problem**  
Forecasts are black-box/absent; impact of content/price/IAP is guesswork.

**Value**  
Explainable 90-day forecasts with backtests & scenarios; +5–15% promo ROI.

**Who**  
Primary: Live Ops Director  
Secondary: PM, Finance BP

**Goals**  
Transparent backtests; editable levers; downloadable plans

**Non-goals**  
Player-level uplift attribution (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Baseline with bands** → Success: bands + drivers shown; MAPE displayed  
- **Must — Scenario compare** → Success: lever values & expected lift exported  
- **Should — Degrade-accuracy alert** → Success: alert triggered; model retrain queued  
- **Could — Calendar overlays** → Success: release/seasonality modifiers visible

**KPIs**  
MAPE visible by horizon; scenario adoption ≥ 60% of Live Ops titles/month

---

### 4.5 Playsage: Launch Control
**Problem**  
Launches and events collide with major beats; attention gets cannibalized; UA costs spike.

**Value**  
Quantified collision risk and safer windows; ≥30% fewer collisions.

**Who**  
Primary: Publishing Director/EP  
Secondary: Marketing Lead, Live Ops

**Goals**  
Explainable risk score (proximity, scale, audience overlap, seasonality); one-click “Find safer windows” with Δrisk & rationale

**Non-goals**  
CPI forecasting (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Window scan**  
  Trigger: date selection → Steps: view 60-day heatmap; click hot cell → drivers → Success: drivers sum to risk ±2 tolerance  
- **Must — Safer suggestions**  
  Trigger: risk > threshold → Steps: click “Find safer windows” → see ≥3 options with Δrisk → Success: option adopted or escalated  
- **Should — Subscriptions**  
  Trigger: competitor shifts → Steps: subscribe → Success: alert ≤ 15m  
- **Could — Internal events overlay** → Success: alignment with owned beats

**KPIs**  
P95 calendar ≤ 2.0s; alert ≤ 15m; % launches moved due to insight; Δrevenue vs baseline

---

### 4.6 Playsage: Watchtower
**Problem**  
Teams get notified too late or get spammed by noisy rules.

**Value**  
Right-sized alerts and digests across KPIs, sentiment, risk; 1–3 analyst hours/day saved.

**Who**  
Primary: PM/Analyst  
Secondary: Live Ops, Exec

**Goals**  
Simple rule builder; multi-channel delivery; low FPR via cooldown/dedupe

**Non-goals**  
Advanced anomaly ML (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — KPI threshold rule**: create → test (backfill) → save; Success: ≤60s  
- **Must — Weekly digest**: schedule; Success: delivered & read  
- **Should — Cooldown/noise control**: reduce duplicate alerts; Success: FPR < 10%  
- **Could — Multi-title bundles**: org-level rule sets

**KPIs**  
Delivery ≥ 99%; FPR < 10%; feed P95 ≤ 1.5s

---

### 4.7 Playsage: The Sage
**Problem**  
Teams have data but lack guidance; plans are inconsistent and slow.

**Value**  
Embedded advisor turns signals into next-best actions with ranges & evidence.

**Who**  
Primary: Live Ops Director  
Secondary: PM, CRM Lead

**Goals**  
≥ 3 recommendations/title; ranges with confidence; exportable test templates

**Non-goals**  
ASO fixes; bug triage prompts

**Use cases**  
- **Must — 2-sprint plan**: ask; receive prioritized actions with sources & ranges → Success: plan exported  
- **Must — Test template**: include KPIs, guardrails, stop rules → Success: handed to production/CRM  
- **Should — Outcome tracking**: acceptance & realized lift → Success: feedback loops  
- **Could — Org policy constraints**: apply caps/floors automatically

**KPIs**  
Coverage ≥ 3 recs/title; P95 latency ≤ 2s; acceptance rate tracked

---

### 4.8 Playsage: Sight
**Problem**  
Execs need a presenter-ready live view; teams waste time reformatting.

**Value**  
Six-tile default, presenter mode, one-click export; consistent narrative.

**Who**  
Primary: GM/VP/CEO  
Secondary: PM leads

**Goals**  
Default six tiles; presenter mode; branded export

**Non-goals**  
Public share links (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Default deck**: load six tiles; Success: P95 ≤ 2s  
- **Must — Export**: PDF/PNG/PPT; Success: brand compliant  
- **Should — Presets**: org default saved; Success: adopted by execs  
- **Could — Presenter controls**: keyboard → focus flow

**KPIs**  
Load P95 ≤ 2s; export ≤ 3s; preset adoption ≥ 70%

---

### 4.9 Playsage: Merchant
**Problem**  
Pricing changes ship without net-impact visibility under evolving policies; affordability opaque.

**Value**  
Simulate fees/taxes/elasticity/affordability with guardrails & overrides.

**Who**  
Primary: Monetization Lead/Commercial Director  
Secondary: Live Ops, Finance BP

**Goals**  
Single policy truth; simulate < 2s; enforce floors/caps

**Non-goals**  
Country-level affordability (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Policy toggle & simulate**: Apple-EU/Google-choice → net updates instantly  
- **Must — Floors/caps**: block illegal pricing; explain error  
- **Should — Overrides**: per-title with audit  
- **Could — Sale planning**: export price plan

**KPIs**  
100% price changes simulated pre-ship; variance vs plan at 14d < 10%; pricing reversals ↓ 50%

---

### 4.10 Playsage: Playermap
**Problem**  
Overlap is guessed from anecdotes; lookalikes are missed.

**Value**  
Interpretable clusters & overlaps drive UA, bundles, positioning.

**Who**  
Primary: UA Lead/PMM  
Secondary: BizDev, PM

**Goals**  
Stable clusters with interpretable labels; export lookalikes

**Non-goals**  
Player-level graph (v1)

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Cluster cards**: size/growth/tags/price band → Success: selected lookalikes exported  
- **Should — Overlap matrix export**: CSV/PNG → Success: used by UA/creatives  
- **Could — Movement over time**: track cluster drift

**KPIs**  
P95 ≤ 2s; stability ≥ 30d; ≥ 5 lookalikes/flagship

---

### 4.11 Playsage: OrgSight (optional add-on)
**Problem**  
Org cadence & health tracked in spreadsheets; weak linkage to outcomes.

**Value**  
Light diagnostics & action plans aligned to advisory; faster alignment.

**Who**  
Primary: CEO/Studio Head  
Secondary: Production Director

**Goals**  
Simple, non-personal indices; actionable plans; clean exports

**Non-goals**  
Employee-level analytics

**Use cases**  
- **Must — Diagnostic run**: indices with definitions; action plan with owners/dates → Success: PDF pack  
- **Should — Monthly cadence**: refresh & review  
- **Could — Outcome link**: correlate to content delivery quality

**KPIs**  
Pack export < 3s; leadership adoption ≥ 70%

---

## 5. Cross-cutting success metrics
- Weekly active decision-makers (Exec/Publishing/Live Ops) ≥ 70% of target by month 3  
- Median time-to-insight < 5 minutes for Marketwatch/Arena/Launch Control  
- Forecast accuracy (MAPE) visible in-app by horizon; degradation alerts on  
- Export usage ≥ 50% of exec sessions; exports are on-brand without editing

## 6. Release plan & milestones
- **M1 (Foundations)**: Marketwatch, Arena (baseline), Sight defaults; exports; provenance labels  
- **M2 (Signal depth)**: Pulse, Launch Control, Watchtower; alerting; saved views/presets  
- **M3 (Decide & simulate)**: Foresight (scenarios), Merchant, Playermap, The Sage; org rollout

## 7. Risks & mitigations
- Rank→DAU uncertainty → **Mitigation**: label Estimated, show provenance, conservative calibration  
- Similarity false positives (Arena/Playermap) → **Mitigation**: manual peer controls, explain-why cards  
- Incomplete release calendars (Launch Control) → **Mitigation**: editor inputs, partner feeds, coverage badges  
- Policy drift (Merchant) → **Mitigation**: versioned fee tables, “needs review” badges

## 8. Packaging (proposal)
- **Core**: Marketwatch, Arena, Sight  
- **Growth**: Core + Pulse, Launch Control, Watchtower  
- **Pro**: Growth + Foresight, Merchant, Playermap, The Sage  
- **Add-on**: OrgSight  
Pricing: per-seat + data tier (TBD with GTM)

# Create an expanded, non-reductive Volume I with deeper Problem & Value narratives.
# Professional formatting; one document only.
from docx import Document
from docx.enum.text import WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH
from docx.shared import Pt
from datetime import datetime

TS = datetime.utcnow().strftime("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M UTC")
OUT = f"/mnt/data/Playsage_Volume_I_ProductPlan_PRD_Expanded_{datetime.utcnow().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.docx"

doc = Document()
# Base styles
style = doc.styles['Normal']
style.font.name = 'Calibri'
style.font.size = Pt(11)

def H(txt, level=1, center=False):
    h = doc.add_heading(txt, level=level)
    if center:
        h.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER
    return h

def P(txt):
    return doc.add_paragraph(txt)

# Cover
H("Playsage — Volume I: Product Plan & PRD", 0, center=True)
p = P(TS); p.alignment = WD_ALIGN_PARAGRAPH.CENTER

# Vision
H("1. Product vision", 1)
P("Playsage is an operator-first decision suite for game studios and publishers. It consolidates market context, competitive intelligence, player sentiment, forecasting with scenarios, release-window risk, alerts, executive reporting, pricing/IAP economics, audience overlaps, and (optionally) organizational diagnostics. The north star is faster, defensible decisions with measurable outcomes—fewer meetings, fewer surprises, more predictable growth.")

# Personas
H("2. Personas", 1)
P("Executives (CEO/GM/VP), Publishing Director/Executive Producer, Live Ops Director, Product Manager/Analyst, Monetization Lead/Economy Designer, Marketing/UA Lead, Finance Business Partner.")

# Scope
H("3. Scope", 1)
P("Platforms: Steam, PlayStation, Xbox, iOS, Google Play.")
P("Seeded genres: Shooter, Adventure, RPG, Battle Royale, Strategy.")
P("Investor-demo success: P95 tile latency ≤ 3s; visible “Estimated” provenance; forecast backtests; offline forced-cache parity; board-ready exports.")

# Helper to add module with expanded Problem & Value plus PRD sections
def module_block(name, problem_paras, value_paras, personas, jtbd, goals, nongoals, usecases, kpis):
    H(name, 2)
    H("Problem", 3)
    for t in problem_paras:
        P(t)
    H("Why now / Value", 3)
    for t in value_paras:
        P(t)
    H("Primary & secondary personas", 3); P(personas)
    H("Jobs-To-Be-Done", 3)
    for j in jtbd: P(f"• {j}")
    H("Goals", 3)
    for g in goals: P(f"• {g}")
    if nongoals:
        H("Non-goals", 3)
        for ng in nongoals: P(f"• {ng}")
    H("Use cases (must/should/could)", 3)
    for u in usecases: P(f"• {u}")
    H("Success metrics & targets", 3)
    for k in kpis: P(f"• {k}")
    P("")

Got it—here are three stronger, market-ready rewrites. Pick one (or mix lines) and I’ll lock it into the docs.

### Option A — Executive, outcome-first
**Playsage is the decision system for game businesses.** It fuses market telemetry, competitive moves, player voice, forecasting science, launch-window risk, alerting, exec presets, pricing/IAP economics, and audience mapping into a single operator workflow. With provenance on every number and scenarios at your fingertips, publishing, live ops, and leadership move from “what happened?” to “what do we do now?” in minutes—reducing collisions, defending pricing, lifting promo ROI, and replacing slide-building with accountable, measurable choices.

### Option B — Brand voice, action verbs
**See the market. Read the room. Pick the moment.** Playsage gives studios and publishers one pane to sense change, model outcomes, and act. We unify industry context, competitor behavior, player sentiment, forecast models, launch-timing risk, alerts/digests, executive pages, pricing & IAP mechanics, and audience overlaps—so teams choose dates, set prices, plan content, and brief leadership with confidence and proof. The result: fewer misses, faster cycles, compounding growth.

### Option C — Investor-grade, precise
**Playsage is an operator-grade analytics and advisory platform built for games.** We integrate cross-platform market and competitive feeds with sentiment, forecasting and scenario planning, release-window risk scoring, alerting/digests, executive presets, pricing/IAP simulation, and audience overlap. Our promise: answer the “what changed?” and “what now?” questions with sourced, explainable metrics and recommended actions—cutting time-to-decision from days to minutes and improving predictability across launches and live operations.

Want a sharper tagline above it (e.g., “Decisions that ship games” or “From signals to strategy”)? Say the word and I’ll finalize with your pick.
